The Principle for Long-Distance Telephone Calls is Three Minutes Per Call 44

(Nanjing) The Telecommunications Conference resolved that the principle for long-distance telephone calls is three minutes per call. Yan Renguang, Director of the Telecommunications Department, said that this resolution is because the duration of each long-distance telephone call in various countries is three minutes. The same is true for Guangdong, Hong Kong, and other places in China. In the future, when international long-distance calls are connected, it will be difficult if the call durations are different. Moreover, it will also be difficult to calculate when communicating with Guangzhou in China. According to past statistics, most call durations do not exceed three minutes. Therefore, it has been decided that three minutes will be the standard, and it will be implemented after international calls are completed. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Siamese Cabinet Resigns 45

Rubber Restriction Act Rejected by Parliament

Bangkok The Siamese rubber quota, submitted to Parliament today for approval in accordance with the international plan, was rejected by a majority vote. As a result, the government immediately resigned. This development may cause the Siamese King, who is currently traveling in Europe, to return home quickly. The government that has now resigned was formed after the coup on July 1, 1932. The result of the coup was that Siam changed from an autocratic system to a constitutional monarchy. The Siamese Parliament's rejection of the rubber quota has been met with sympathy from the London rubber industry, which believes that Siam's request for a larger quota is justified and expects that the quota will be revised soon to suit the country's production capacity. When rumors of the Siamese Parliament's decision first spread, the London rubber market fell, but the price rebounded after it was not confirmed. The London rubber industry believes that if the Siamese quota is gradually increased, it will not cause a major hindrance to the overall statistics. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

The United States Navy Organizes a Strong Air Force 47

Forty-Six New Aircraft Will Be Available Next Spring

Capable of Flying Hundreds of Miles Away to Destroy Enemy Ships

(Washington) Within months, the United States Navy will have an air force with extremely high speed and range. Of the twenty-three reconnaissance aircraft currently available, some participated in the formation flight from California to Hawaii. After successful tests in this area and Norfolk, they will be formed into a new squadron. In addition, twenty-three of the latest aircraft are being built. The maximum speed of each aircraft flying from California to Hawaii is 130 miles per hour. According to senior naval officials, the speed of the new aircraft is much faster than this. Next spring, the Navy will have forty-six reconnaissance aircraft capable of flying hundreds of miles away to bomb enemy fleets, and these new aircraft can even compete with airships. (National Electric)

United States Arms Investigation 48

Part of the Testimony is Not Released

Fearing International Disputes

(Washington) Part of the testimony obtained by the Senate Committee investigating the arms trade is now prohibited from being released, as at least five countries have protested against the published events. The investigators held a secret meeting with Secretary of State Hull and Secretary of Commerce Roper this morning before continuing the investigation. Chairman Nye then stated that the committee had no intention of being perfunctory and had not received such a request. The committee is now moving forward, and no one has said that the committee is proceeding too hastily. Today, a representative of the Constant Company, Landemote, told the investigation committee that in 1933, the joint representatives of Constant Company and the British company Bunnemann in Shanghai suggested that the two companies should separately negotiate with the United States State Department and the British Foreign Office. Landemote also said that in 1932, he had visited the Deputy Secretary of State with Senator Townsend, and then sold a patented method of manufacturing light gas to Mitsui & Co. for use by Japan. At that time, Mitsui & Co. was engaged in activities similar to war preparations, but Constant Company heard from Mitsui & Co. that this manufacturing method was not of major importance to military purposes. Land also said that Constant Company had received a report that although the Treaty of Versailles prohibited Germany from manufacturing explosives, Germany was still manufacturing large quantities of highly explosive materials. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(Washington) Brazil, Mexico, Argentina, Chile, Bolivia, and other countries may have lodged or are about to lodge strong protests regarding the Senate committee's investigation into arms sales. Secretary of State Hull discussed this matter with Senate Committee Chairman Nye this morning. Although the two said afterward that the investigation would continue and would not slacken, it seems that the committee is proceeding cautiously in view of the protests from various countries. This can be seen from two things: First, a representative of the DuPont arms company in China presented the committee with several letters stating that he had sold arms to China in 1932, and some Chinese officials and generals received commissions. The committee refused to disclose the names of these people, which is evidence of caution. Second, the Argentine government built an arsenal in 1933 and had originally signed a contract with a German company. DuPont lobbied Argentina to cancel the original contract and let DuPont undertake the project. The correspondence regarding this matter was submitted to the committee by the DuPont representative in South America. Committee Chairman Nye said that this telegram could not be published in its entirety, otherwise, "it is feared that it would cause a backlash in the politics of a certain country in the Americas," which is the second evidence that the committee's attitude is gradually becoming more cautious. (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

The Situation of the American Textile Workers' Strike Remains Dangerous 49

The Union Attempts to Test the Strength of the National Recovery Administration through This Strike

Serious Riots Occur in North Carolina

Washington, Providence - Mediation negotiations have completely stalled, so the strike situation is extremely dangerous today. Although the Rhode Island legislature refused yesterday to consider authorizing Governor Green to use troops to protect textile factories, it is now meeting again to reconsider the matter. Serious riots previously occurred in the area of Woonsocket, resulting in two deaths and five injuries, with three of the injured in critical condition and over four hundred with minor injuries. Order is currently being maintained under the bayonet, and a second riot is brewing. (National Telegram, 14th)

(New York) - The strike situation in Rhode Island has eased slightly, but disturbances occurred today in the town of Burlington, North Carolina. The National Guard and demonstrators clashed, as four hundred strikers attempted to prevent a cotton mill from opening. Military police attempted to disperse them, but when that proved ineffective, they used tear gas to achieve their purpose. During the clashes, five demonstrators were bayoneted, fortunately with minor injuries. Four people were arrested. According to many opinions, the union intends to use the strike to test its power over the National Recovery Administration. Some cotton mill owners have admitted in private conversations that other industry leaders are pressuring cotton manufacturers to reject the demands of the textile workers, because if the cotton mills give in, the labor unrest will spread to other industries. According to today's news, the authorities are now considering an order to reduce working hours in factories nationwide without changing wages, in order to ease the current labor unrest. (Reuters, 14th)

(Washington) - Since the textile workers' strike began, General Johnson, head of the National Recovery Administration, spoke for the first time today, saying that before the textile industry code was signed, he had reached an understanding with McMahon, president of the United Textile Workers of America, and that the current strike is a complete violation of that understanding. Gorman, chairman of the strike committee, is currently campaigning among other unions to prevent the import of textiles, in order to strengthen the strike's momentum. The strike committee today called on transportation workers not to handle imported textiles. (Reuters, 15th)

The Investigation of the Morro Castle Disaster Continues 50

(New York) - According to Sullivan, the purser of the "Morro Castle," the ship was carrying 1,000 liters of flammable paint, which made it easy for the fire to spread. Some sailors testified that the ship's lifeboats were not adequately prepared for immediate use, and that the officers did not fulfill their duties, so no orders were issued when the fire broke out. A passenger stated that he glimpsed flames at 12:45 AM, but the radio distress signal was not sent until 3:15 AM. Other passengers said they did not hear any alarm at that time. The federal prosecutor issued a rebuke to the Ward Line, the owner of the ship, saying that it was trying to incite the crew to conceal the truth during questioning, which hindered the investigation. (Havas, 14th)

(New York) - The Congressional committee investigating anti-American propaganda movements has recently decided to expand the scope of its work to include an investigation of the "Morro Castle" disaster. According to witness testimony and news from Havana, some of the ship's crew were leaning towards communism, hence the committee's decision. (Havas, 14th)

(London) - It is rumored here that the investigation of the American mail ship "Morro Castle" disaster will be extended to the United Kingdom. According to the Daily Mail, some people are wanted by American police officers. Local detectives have learned their ages and appearances, and several ships are under surveillance. It is generally believed that news from New York has confirmed that the Morro Castle disaster was due to sabotage. (Havas, 15th)

Australian House of Representatives Re-election 51

Competition Between the United Australia Party and the Labor Party

Canberra - Australia will hold elections for the Central House of Representatives today. The United Australia Party, led by Prime Minister Lyons, is seeking to continue in power to address issues such as rural recovery, commerce, defense, finance, and cooperation with the Empire. Opposing them is the Labor Party. Both sides are confident of victory, but even if the government party loses many seats, it can still form a new government with the support of the Country Party, which sponsors the Prime Minister. (Reuters, 15th)

The Polish Question Eases 52

No Further Diplomatic Action

But There Are Public Demonstrations Domestically

(Geneva) - The general discussion of the League of Nations Assembly has ended. After Polish Foreign Minister Beck expressed his views on the issue of ethnic minorities, he did not request to speak again. Poland's expression does not seem to contain any seriousness. British Foreign Secretary Simon has decided to return to London soon and plans to come back here within the next week. The Polish Foreign Minister plans to explain further when the motion to promote the protection of ethnic minorities is submitted to the Executive Council for discussion, as is the usual League of Nations procedure. League of Nations officials, who were quite shocked when Beck suddenly mentioned this matter, have now changed their minds, and if no accidents occur, people's minds may be stabilized as a result. (Havas, 14th)

Warsaw - The Pat Agency reports that 30,000 people gathered in a square in the center of the capital to express sympathy for Foreign Minister Beck's declaration on the issue of ethnic minorities in Geneva. Many Jewish representatives and war veterans attended. Similar expressions were made in other cities as well. (Havas Agency, 15th)

French Constitutional Reform 53

Premier Doumergue Completes Plan

Restricting the Powers of Members of Parliament to Eliminate Political Turmoil

(Paris) - French Premier Doumergue, while on vacation in Tournefeuille, has been considering important constitutional reforms. Doumergue will now take his plan back to Paris. He advocates restricting the powers of members of parliament so that governments cannot be overthrown and reorganized without a general election. Doumergue has always admired the British system and is now adopting it. (Reuters, 14th)

Mussolini Suddenly Arrives in Venice 54

Meets with Austrian Politicians

The Contents of the Meeting Remain Secret

British Naval Admiral Arrives Simultaneously

French Foreign Minister's Visit to Italy Undecided

Venice - Italian Premier Mussolini and Austrian Education Minister and other leaders are now here, ostensibly to attend a concert, but many believe that their real purpose must be elsewhere and that important events are awaiting resolution. This afternoon, the Italian Premier met with three Austrian politicians on his yacht "Aurora" for a long conversation. Everything was kept strictly secret, which made it even more noticeable. It is noted that the Italian Premier met with Hitler here several months ago. (Reuters, 14th)

Venice - British Naval Admiral Turner arrived here aboard the warship "London." Today, Turner hosted Premier Mussolini on the ship. (Havas, 14th)

(Paris) - Foreign Minister Barthou will visit Rome in the autumn to meet with Italian Premier Mussolini, but the date of the visit has not yet been decided. Various reports on this matter are inaccurate. (Havas, 14th)

The Spanish Cabinet Struggles on 55

Resignation is Almost Inevitable

Madrid - The Spanish Samper Cabinet, which was originally scheduled to submit its resignation on Sunday, decided today to postpone it temporarily. However, because the current cabinet has lost the support of the parliamentary majority party, resignation is ultimately unavoidable. However, Parliament is scheduled to reconvene on October 1st. Although the current cabinet has decided to make a final struggle, political circles still anticipate that the current cabinet will fall first. The current cabinet is doing its best to maintain order, and all kinds of political demonstrations are prohibited. (National Telegram, 15th)

Japan Prepares to Start Trade Negotiations with Portugal and Australia 56

The New Indo-Japanese Trade Agreement Has Been Implemented Effectively

(Tokyo) - The Portuguese government previously notified the Japanese government of the termination of the Japan-Portugal Treaty of Commerce and Navigation. However, according to a telegram from Chargé d'Affaires Tsumakibe of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Portuguese government intends to negotiate a new treaty with Japan and will begin negotiations in Lisbon on the 20th. (Japan United Press, 15th)

(Tokyo) - The Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now drafted a Japan-Australia trade treaty and will soon propose negotiations to the Australian government. When drafting the original text of the treaty, the government gave special consideration to Japan-Australia trade relations and Japan's industrial policy in order to promote Japan's foreign trade. (Japan United Press, 13th)

(Tokyo) - According to a telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs from Ambassador Matsudaira stationed in the United Kingdom, Matsudaira notified the British government on the 14th that the Japanese government had approved the Japan-India trade treaty, so this treaty will be officially implemented from the 14th. (Japan United Press, 15th)

Japan Massively Purchases Iron Raw Materials from Abroad 57

The Import Volume of Iron Scrap Increases Sharply

(Tokyo) - Japan's iron and steel industry remains busy this year. According to a survey by the Japan Iron & Steel Co., Ltd., from January to July of this year, the import of iron scrap from abroad reached 700,000 metric tons. After July, the import volume has increased further. If futures are included, the total amount of iron scrap this year could reach 1.5 million metric tons. The reason for this is that Japan lacks pig iron, so it uses iron scrap to manufacture steel. The import volume this year is much higher than the 1.04 million metric tons last year and 550,000 metric tons the year before, which has attracted considerable attention in industrial and business circles for its future prospects. (Japan United Press, 15th)

Japan Seeks Further Economic Control over Manchukuo 58

Plans to Establish a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference

Full Reform Plan to Be Implemented Next Year

(Tokyo) - Regarding the issue of the Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Army Ministry are focusing on studying the details of its structure. The basic guidelines are as follows: (1) In order to promote Japan-Manchukuo economic cooperation and review the business supervision of special joint Japan-Manchukuo ventures, and to make timely recommendations to the governments of both countries, a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference will be permanently established in Changchun. (2) This conference will be established by treaty between the two countries and will be under the supervision of the governments of both countries. (3) This conference will be composed of an equal number of members appointed by the governments of both countries, and the chairman will be elected by the members. (Dentsu, 15th)

The Military Department Ruling Manchukuo Seeks to Seize Real Power 59

(Tokyo) - The personnel for the newly established Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs are now awaiting the legalization of the decided reform plan. The Cabinet and the Army Ministry will strengthen coordination, but the Army focuses on substance, not form, so its views on the Bureau are as follows:

(1) The Bureau's excessive powers may lead to duplication of effort in its relationship with the Army. Therefore, it is desirable that active-duty military personnel fill any position as Director-General or Deputy Director-General. (2) When adopting a "Grand Director-General" system with a minister-level figure serving as Director-General, it is appropriate to have a major general-level active-duty military officer serve as Deputy Director-General to be in charge of substantive matters. (3) If the Director-General holds real power, a lieutenant general-level active-duty military officer should be appointed, and a civilian official should be appointed as Deputy Director-General, etc. Therefore, it is more strongly opposed to adopting a "Grand Director-General" system to expand the organization of the Bureau than the balance between the military commander of the ambassador with full powers and the Minister of the Army. (Dentsu, 15th)

(Tokyo) - The Japanese government passed the reform plan for the Manchukuo organs on the 14th. However, regarding the Director-General and Deputy Director-General of the Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs directly under the Cabinet, the government advocates appointing a military officer as Director-General and an active-duty military officer as Deputy Director-General, but the military department advocates appointing a civilian official as Director-General and a military officer as Deputy Director-General, allowing the Deputy Director-General to hold real power. However, its advocacy is not strong, and it also reveals the intention of appointing a powerful figure who can understand the actual situation in Manchuria as Deputy Director-General. (Kahren News Agency, 10th)

(Tokyo) - The most noteworthy aspects of the reform plan for the organs stationed in Manchukuo, which was decided by the Cabinet meeting yesterday, are the organization of the Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs and the concurrent appointment of the Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army as the Director of the Administrative Affairs Bureau. According to its regulations, (1) one of the Director-General or section chiefs of the Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs shall be filled by an incumbent military officer; (2) it shall be clearly stipulated by order that the Chief of Staff of the Army shall concurrently serve as the Director of the Bureau of Administrative Affairs when necessary; (3) when the Counselor of the Embassy concurrently serves as the Director of the Bureau of Administrative Affairs, the Counselor shall be primarily responsible for foreign-related matters, consular affairs, and foreign ceremonies. (Japan United Press, 15th)

Koiso Has the Highest Voice for the Director-General Position 60

(Tokyo) - For the sake of implementing its policy towards Manchukuo, the Cabinet has established the Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs. Because it is necessary to have close contact with the various organs stationed in Manchukuo, it has decided to appoint a current army general as its Director-General. The most promising candidate is Lieutenant General Koiso Kuniaki, the current commander of the 5th Division. Other candidates also being mentioned are Lieutenant General Yanagawa Heisuke, commander of the 1st Division, and Lieutenant General Tatekawa Yoshitsugu, commander of the 10th Division. (Japan United Press, 15th)

The Military Department Is Eager for the Implementation of the Reform 61

Due to Budgetary Reasons, the Bureau Will Be Established First

(Tokyo) - The reform plan for the organs in Manchukuo is generally scheduled to be implemented from April of next year. However, the Army hopes to realize it within this year. Although full implementation is relatively difficult, it expects rapid implementation of what can be implemented under this year's budget or what is not related to the budget. Therefore, the government will accommodate the demand to a considerable extent and intends to first engage in the formation of the Bureau of Manchukuo Affairs. (Dentsu, 15th)

The Kwantung Government Is Indignant, and Executives Adopt a Cautious Approach 62

(Dalian) - After the Kwantung Government received the telegram from the Ministry of Colonial Affairs late last night regarding the decision on the reform plan, Chief of Internal Affairs Bureau Hika and other executives immediately convened a meeting. Police Chief Oba, who is currently in Tokyo, also sent a telegram instructing them to be patient and careful and to stay at their posts. Therefore, the attitude of the leadership seems to be inclined to observe the situation temporarily and make plans for a proper solution. Therefore, this morning at 10:00, all government officials gathered in the meeting room, where Chief Hika reported the situation and expressed the hope that everyone would be self-disciplined. (Dentsu, 15th)

(Tokyo) - The 10,000 employees of the Kwantung Government have become indignant because the reform plan of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs was not adopted, and they have decided to resign en masse and submit their resignations. The Army is deeply regretful about this issue, considering that the duties in Manchukuo cannot be neglected even for a day due to the actual situation, and the Kwantung Government employees have actually taken this action, which will have a major impact on security. Therefore, it sincerely hopes that the police officers of the Kwantung Government will exercise self-restraint, and in order to prepare for any eventuality, the Kwantung Army Command and the central department are studying how to fill the security gaps. Therefore, a security plan has recently been completed. (Dentsu, 15th)

(Dalian) - More than 10,000 officials of the Kwantung Government have expressed dissatisfaction with the government's compromise plan to reform the Manchukuo organs. Yesterday, they held a committee meeting, vowed to unite as one from beginning to end, and issued a statement opposing the compromise plan: (1) Oppose the constitutional police system; (2) Hope for a civil service system for the Director-General; (3) Oppose the military department taking control of the supervisory power of the South Manchuria Railway; (4) Oppose the diplomaticization of the administration of the affiliated areas. (Dentsu, 15th)

British Delegation Departs for Berlin Today

(London) - It has been officially announced that Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the Treasury's chief economic advisor, is scheduled to travel to Berlin on Sunday to discuss trade issues between the two countries with the German government, seeking to reach an agreement that will satisfy British exporters. If these negotiations are not successful, the British government will adopt a clearing system for all trade between the United Kingdom and Germany. (Havas, 14th)

Müller's order is intended to ensure absolute obedience from all church officials. This order also applies to church administrators and personnel in all dioceses. Shanghai Merchants Obtain Three Brokerage Seats

Gold and Silver 70

London Bullion - The price of gold in London today was 140 shillings and 5 pence, down one and a half pence.

London Silver - The London silver market has risen due to purchases from the United States and India. Spot rose 1.25 and futures rose 0.0625, both to 21 pence 8125. China sold, and the market is stable.

Bombay Silver - The Bombay silver market remains quiet. The price rose by one anna. Spot is 60 rupees and 5 annas, October term is 60 rupees and 5 annas, and November term is 60 rupees and 7 annas.

Exchange Rates 71

British-American - The London foreign exchange market was sluggish this morning. The opening exchange rate between British and American currency was $5.009375, which was 0.0001875 lower than the closing exchange rate between American and British currency yesterday. The price remained unchanged at the close. Also, one US dollar equals three shillings, eleven pence and 911 ten-thousandths of a pound.

British-French - The opening price was 75 francs and 06 centimes, the same as yesterday's closing price. It fell three pounds in the eleventh hour and rose six pounds at noon to 75 francs and 09 centimes. The price remained unchanged at the close.

American-British - The New York foreign exchange market was stagnant this morning. The opening exchange rate between American and British currency was down 0.000125 to $5.01. The price remained unchanged at the time of transmission.

Cotton and Wheat 72

American Cotton - The New York cotton market did not move at the opening. Subsequently, the price fell slightly due to some hedging sales. As the price fell, buying interest arose. The reason for this was the influence of the government's 1.2 cent loan and the speculation that the power of the textile industry strike was weakening. However, many parties settled in large quantities, causing the market price to fall sharply. The price at 10:40 AM was four pounds lower than the opening price.

Indian Cotton - The Bombay cotton market initially rose due to the replenishment of shorts and purchases by European merchants, and then fell due to profit-taking by bulls. The closing price for white cotton of the April-May term was 216 rupees and 25, down one and a half rupees.

British Cotton - The price in the Liverpool cotton market also fell today. The closing price for the October term was 6.80, down three pounds from yesterday.

British Wheat - The closing price for the October term in the Liverpool wheat market today fell 0.375 to 5 shillings and 7 pence and 0.25.

American Wheat - The wheat market opened today down between 0.375 and 0.625. Large-scale imports of wheat have shaken the wheat market, but the wheat market is fundamentally strong, and the recent price has risen between 0.25 and 0.375.

Rubber 73

New York - After the sharp drop yesterday, the rubber market rebounded today. The price rebounded by about seven pounds at the opening, and then rose another three pounds. However, due to profit-taking, the price fell slightly. The price at 10:40 AM was one pound higher than the opening price.

Securities 74

The market was sluggish at the opening this morning, with the price of various stocks falling from zero to one pound. American steel preferred stock fell by two pounds. Ministry of Communications Sets Regulations for Ship Licensing 78

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has separately established three regulations for ship licensing, stipulating that certificates or licenses will be issued for the following types of routes: (1) those applying for certificates when no ships are currently operating; (2) inland river routes with no existing disputes; (3) existing ship routes that have not been changed. These regulations have been issued to all maritime affairs offices for compliance. (15th Dispatch)

Qimen County Magistrate Lu Ziming Escorted to Anqing 92

Excellent Autumn Silkworm Results in Shandong Province 93

(Hangzhou) The National Sericulture Improvement Association established two autumn silkworm guidance centers in Linqu, Shandong Province, this autumn to guide the experimental rearing of autumn silkworms. According to reports from the centers, the young silkworms are developing extremely well, with the earliest nearing their third molt. The work is expected to be completed before the end of this month. The association believes that Shandong Province's climate is highly suitable for silkworm rearing. Investigations show that the province can produce approximately 10,000 piculs of silk annually, but most are inferior varieties with poor quality. The association plans to use over 1.3 million sheets of improved varieties next year to carry out improvements. (15th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Joint Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Factory Issue 94

(Hangzhou) On the morning of the 15th, the National Sericulture Improvement Association specially invited several representatives from Jiangsu and Zhejiang factories to discuss methods for raising capital for the proposed joint Jiangsu-Zhejiang silk factory. It is reported that opinions were not unanimous, and the establishment date remains to be determined. (15th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Zhejiang Pest Control Personnel All Dismissed 95

(Hangzhou) All pest control personnel in Zhejiang Province have been dismissed to save expenses. All pest control administration in each county will be managed by the district agricultural farms, if such exist. Otherwise, one to three people will be selected from the original pest control personnel to be retained in the central counties of each prefecture. Hereafter, the total pest control expenses will be approximately over 100,000 yuan per year, and counties cannot use these funds without approval from the provincial government. (15th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Orders 96

Order of the National Government on the 14th: Wang Zhengji, Political Vice Minister of the Auditing Department, has submitted his resignation. Wang Zhengji is hereby approved to be relieved of his current position. This order. Also, Mei Zhezhi, Director of General Affairs of the Ministry of Industry, is appointed to another position. Mei Zhezhi should be relieved of his current position. This order. Also, Yan Jiguang is appointed to act as Director of General Affairs of the Ministry of Industry on a trial basis. This order.

Order of the National Government on the 15th: Liu Zhenhua, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region, has submitted his resignation. Liu Zhenhua is hereby approved to be relieved of his concurrent post. This order. Also, bandit suppression matters in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border region shall be directly commanded by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. All the Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border region should be abolished immediately. This order.

Guangdong, Chaozhou, and Meixian Counties Change to Levy Provisional Land Tax 101

It is also reported that the Financial Department recently received secret reports from the people that the current land tax in various counties is levied as high as six or seven yuan per mu. The names of the items and the sources and uses of the funds are not stated and are not submitted to higher-level agencies for approval. The Financial Department has dispatched multiple secret investigators to various counties to investigate the amount of embezzlement and its use due to the unauthorized actions of local agencies. Moreover, the abolition of cash grain and the handling of local guards have been carried out vigorously in the inland counties. Robust men are drawn for training from time to time, and graduates from the Yantang Military Academy are transferred to various armies as platoon leaders. Anhui Salt Transfer Shore Dispute 102

Provincial Government Resolves to Stop Datong Workers from Intercepting Transportation

Transportation Office Builds Central Salt Warehouse in Datong

Wuhu Correspondence: The transfer of Anhui Huai salt's guiding shores from Datong to Anqing has led Datong loading and unloading workers to gather thousands of people to block river transportation, fearing its impact on their livelihoods, creating a severe situation. The Wuhu Anhui Shore Transportation Bureau, fearing the expansion of the dispute and the occurrence of accidents, specially sent General Affairs Section Chief Yu Quji to the provincial capital to negotiate solutions with the provincial government. Mr. Yu returned to Wuhu yesterday. The provincial government is determined to maintain responsibility for the 200 tickets of Huai salt being transported to Anqing and has telegraphed the Tongling County Government and the Datong Public Security Bureau to stop the Datong salt workers from gathering to cause disturbances at any time and to prevent them from acting out of line. Therefore, the transfer of Huai salt to Anqing should not cause further problems recently. On the one hand, to help Datong workers and the market, the Transportation Office has decided to build a central salt warehouse in Tong. The scope of the warehouse is extremely large. The benefits to the Datong market in the future will be even greater than before. They have now purchased the former Shuili Bureau's building as the warehouse site. Once the handover is clear, construction can begin. The Transportation Bureau has also announced the reasons for setting up a warehouse in Anqing and the measures for relief in Datong. It is claimed that Anqing is 180 li from Datong, while Qianshan, Dongliu, Taihu, Wangjiang, Zhizhi, and Susong counties upstream are even further from Tong. In the past, due to the regulations, Anqing was not allowed to open a shore for salt sales, and these counties had to travel hundreds of miles to purchase salt. Since last winter and spring, the Transportation Office changed to transport 50 tickets of Huai salt by inland waterway directly to Anqing for trial sales. People in the upstream counties were delighted by the convenience of daily consumption. When the trial salt was sold out, Zhang Yinmosen, chairman of the Huaining County Chamber of Commerce, and Xu Leisheng and other representatives of the seven counties, repeatedly telegraphed to request continued operation of Anqing's water transport to benefit the people's food supply. This is the actual situation of the people's food supply. The merchants and people of the upstream seven counties are unwilling to go to Tong to buy salt due to geographical restrictions. Moreover, Taihu County borders Yingshan and Huoshan counties in Anhui and Henan provinces, and Zhizhi County borders Qimen in Zhejiang. Therefore, before the central salt warehouse in Datong is completed, in order to stabilize the food supply of the upstream counties and save the declining tax revenue, it is necessary to set up a salt warehouse in Anqing to avoid the opportunity for cheap salt from Anhui, Henan, and Zhejiang to rush into the market. After the completion of the Datong central general warehouse, all salt in Tongling, Qingyang, Shitai, Guichi, Huaining, Qianshan, Susong, Wangjiang, Taihu, Zhizhi, and Tongcheng counties can be taxed and released from the warehouse. Datong's future prosperity will be ten times greater than today. (13th)

Dangerous River Situation in Wuzhi, Henan Province 103

Many Cave-ins at Kaifeng North Flood Control Second Dam

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Xia Kuajiao of the Qi Baotou Dam under the jurisdiction of the Wenwu Flood Seven Forts in the Yellow River in Henan Province was washed away by backflow water from 10 PM to 12 PM on the 9th, with a cave-in of more than a zhang. The earth core has been exposed, and the situation is dangerous. The Shangbei Sub-bureau immediately instructed the target soldiers to rush to protect it. However, the river situation in Wuzhi Flood River has also been changing at any moment recently. The top impact point goes up and down from time to time, and the situation is dangerous. The top impact point of the second dam of the Five Forts moved at noon on the 10th, and the Xia Kuajiao was cave-in. Also, one stone pile on the lower head of the earth dam of the Six Forts and two stone piles on the upper head of the seventh dam of the Eight Forts were all eroded by the flood and exposed the cave-in. In addition to supervising the target soldiers and hiring coolies to move stone squares for protection and resistance, the Shangbei Sub-bureau specifically telegraphed the Yellow River Affairs General Bureau to report the emergency. Also, engineer Zheng Yaoxi telegraphed the Yellow River Commission, saying that the water level had dropped in recent days, the river situation had risen, and the main stream was directly impacting the nineteenth fort six dams and the twentieth fort head two dams in Kaifeng North Flood, but it was not as tense as the previous days, and lead wire cages had been used to load stones and fortify it. However, the height was insufficient. If there is no major flood, it will be sufficient to resist. The new stones from Gongxian were shipped in two boats on the 6th, but there have been no more shipments to date. All other projects are quite stable. (12th)

Shandong Library Newly Purchases Bronze Vessels of the Wu Family of Hai feng 104

Will Compile and Publish Illustrated Catalogue of Bronze Vessels of the Haiyue Lou

Jinan Correspondence: The Wu family of Haifeng (now Wudi) has the largest private collection of ancient bronzes in Shandong. It started with Wu Zibi (Shifen), and his son Zhongyi continued it. With high ranks and generous salaries, several generations were serially linked. At the same time, Xu Yinlin and Chen Fuzhai and others were appraising it. All bronze vessels, precious seals, clay seals, bricks, tiles, and stone inscriptions were the richest collection. Their seals have been copied into the Shuangyu Hu Zhai Yin Cun. The clay seals have been compiled with Chen's "Examination of Clay Seals." There are also "Jugu Jinwen" and "Shiwen" two books. The "Jinwen" in nine volumes is the richest collection of bronze vessel inscriptions, and the textual research is also very accurate, which is known at home and abroad. The collected bronzes have been prepared for inclusion in the "Jugu Lu Jinwen". The house has ten halls, known as the Ten Rooms. All gold and stone literary objects are stored in the rooms. Wu Zhongyi has been an official in Henan for a long time, and no one in his family manages them. His servants sometimes stole gold and stone from the rooms for sale. The golden Buddha given by Empress Dowager Cixi was also among the stolen items. Later, Wu Zhongyi was dismissed from office and returned home. Fearing that he would thoroughly investigate the lost items, the family burned the Ten Rooms, falsely claiming that it was a divine fire. All the gold, stone, and heavy objects were turned into ashes. After the house was burned, they counted the remaining gold and stones and still hid them at home. In the spring of this year, a part of the bronzes suddenly wandered into the Jinan market. After the Provincial Library learned about it, they purchased them in many ways. After two months, all the scattered bronzes were successively included in the library, a total of twenty-two pieces, all with inscriptions. Twenty pieces are seen in the "Jugu Lu". The remaining two Han artifacts are seen in the "Qin Han Jinwen Lu" and other books. Unfortunately, after being burned, the color is no longer the same as before, and there may be some damage. The molten gold juice is sometimes on the device. Fortunately, the inscriptions are complete. The Shi Jun Fu is the best. The museum now plans to collect about a hundred pieces of bronze ware with inscriptions collected before and after and compile them into a collection of Haiyue Lou Yiqi catalogues. Recently, in addition to receiving a part of the Wu family, it has also purchased ten newly unearthed bronzes from various places and two sections of the Han Xiping Stone Classics, all of which are valuable. Now I will explore and record the catalogue of each device separately.

(A) Newly Collected Remnants of Burned Bronze Vessels of the Wu Family of Haifeng (1) Shi Jun Fu, (2) Yuan Fu Dun, (3) Ce Fu Yi Ding, (4) Dong Fu Bing Jue, (5) Ri Ren Lu Gai, (6) Chang Tang Yi, (7) Fu Dun, (8) Ling Yi, (9) Ming Wo Ding, (10) Zang Bo Ding, (11) Qi Bo Min Fu Dun Gai, (12) Feng Jue, (13) Zi Sun Jue, (14) Yu Bei Jue, (15) Fu Xin Jue One, (16) Fu Xin Jue Two, (17) Bei Fu Yi Jue, (18) Nai Yi Jue, (19) Fu Xin Zhi, (all of the above are seen in "Jugu Lu Jinwen"), (20) Han Nanpi Hou Jia Ding, (21) Zhong of the fourth year of the Han Yongchu, (22) Bottom of a Qianqiu Hu of the Han Dynasty (all of the above are seen in the "Qin Han Jinwen Lu" and other books)

(B) Newly Unearthed Bronze Vessels with Inscriptions Collected in Recent Years (1) Gui Fu Jue, (2) Dong Zu Gui Jue, (3) Wu Dun, (4) Jiang Yu Gu, (5) Zi Qi Yangwen Jue, (6) Zang Ge, (7) Yin Ge, (8) Situ Ge, (9) Zhou Ding (There are four lines of text, about forty or fifty characters, mostly incomplete and unrecognizable), (10) Dong Ge (All the above refer to those with inscriptions, and those without inscriptions are not recorded.)

(C) Han Stone Classics Han Xiping Stone Classics Shangshu Lu Shi, a total of two stones, seventy characters. (The museum purchased more than eighty stones of Han and Wei stone classics from Luoyang last year, purchased more than thirty stones this spring, and finally collected these two stones, with more characters. The stone has been copied into a book early, and the proofreading, printing and narrative have been completed, and the book will be published soon.)

Qingpu 105

The library has also purchased a new masterpiece. Some students from Baihejiang Town, in the northern township of the county, collected money to purchase a set of "Wanyou Wenku" in the autumn of the eighteenth year, and then initiated the organization of a library to store books. In the autumn of the nineteenth year, they raised funds and then recruited workers to build library houses. In April of the twentieth year, the library houses were completed, and the opening ceremony was held, and it was named Qingpu County No. 1 Library. At the time of the opening, in addition to the Wanyou Wenku, the masterpiece books also borrowed all the twenty-four histories of the Haiqin Lou Collection, and all the four collections of the Yangsu Xuan Collection of the Zhonghua Book Company, as well as other magazines, novels, jurisprudence, medicine, etc., were available. In the twenty-first year, they raised money again to purchase all the four series of books from the Commercial Press. In the twenty-second year, in order to promote the sages and add glory to the town, they added plates to the two masterpieces "Xiting Wenchao" written by Wang Yuan, and "Song Bin Quan Ji" written by Xu Xiqi, and published them into books, which were donated to universities, etc. to exchange books to increase culture. Recently, they have raised huge sums of money to subscribe to the entire "Gujin Tushu Jicheng," which will be published by the Zhonghua Book Company. With a library with an annual recurring expenditure of less than 400 yuan, can purchase masterpieces every year. The enthusiasm of local people for culture can be seen here.

The route of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway was designated at the beginning of the construction of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. Wuxi 109

Tobacco Exchange Appeals Against Tax Increase

Various shops in this county, including soy sauce and wine businesses, wine and soy sauce shops, tobacco exchanges, cigarette businesses, and native tobacco businesses, have traditionally entrusted their respective trade associations to pay the tobacco and alcohol license taxes to the tax office on their behalf. This autumn, the shops followed the usual practice of submitting the tax payments and old licenses to their respective trade associations for collective payment. However, the director of the tax office, Zhu Jinzhang, demanded that the tax amount for this season be doubled compared to previous years, which led to no result. The trade associations then returned the tax payments and old licenses to their respective member shops, instructing them to go to the tax office to pay on their own. When the shops, following the tax amount of previous years, went to the tax office with the payments and old licenses, they were all detained by the tax office, which sparked a backlash. The shops reported the situation to their respective trade associations for assistance. The trade associations, considering the severe drought and the economic downturn in all industries, believed that the tax office was disregarding the hardship of businesses and imposing exorbitant levies that merchants and the public could not afford. Therefore, they submitted petitions to Party and government institutions and organizations, requesting relief. Yesterday, more than one hundred tobacco exchange shops, including Fuxing, stated that Zhu Jinzhang is actually a pseudonym of Zhu Jin, who originally made his fortune by handling taxes and regards exploiting tobacco and alcohol merchants as his only means of accumulating wealth. Today, what he enjoys and squanders are all the blood and sweat of tobacco and alcohol merchants, treating them as meat on his chopping board and fish in his pot. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and disasters are frequent, and the people are struggling to survive, Zhu Jinzhang disregards the lives of the people, imposes exorbitant levies, and only cares about his own family's happiness, ignoring the suffering of others. The merchants and the public cannot afford this illegal tax increase. Therefore, they jointly petitioned the tobacco exchange association to appeal for relief, vowing to perish together if their goal is not achieved, and submitted the tax payments and old licenses for this season to the trade association for safekeeping. The situation is extremely serious. At the same time, the Wujin tobacco exchange industry, because the director of the tobacco and alcohol license tax collection office in that county, Zhu Gu, is also a pseudonym of Zhu Jinzhang and also uses the pseudonym Zhao Qian, who also holds the position of director of the fourth district of the Jiangsu Province Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau, illegally imposed exorbitant levies and enriched himself at the expense of the people. Therefore, they filed a complaint with the provincial bureau. The provincial government has now dispatched Commissioner Lu Baoxi to Changzhou to investigate and handle the matter, it is said.

Local News

Continuous Autumn Rain in This City for Days, Even Heavier Last Night 118

Low-Lying Roads Flooded, Knee-Deep

Fortunately, No High Tide, Water Recedes Quickly

Wall Collapse on Zhoujiazui Road Injures People

The recent continuous autumn rain is reminiscent of the plum rain season. Yesterday morning around 10:00 AM, there was a heavy downpour, with alternating periods of rain and cessation. The rain became even heavier in the evening. As of this morning, the rain has not stopped. Low-lying areas on various roads have turned into swamps. The water depth on North Sichuan Road, Laobazi Road, Zhejiang Road, and other places is about a foot deep. Fortunately, there were no hurricanes or high tides yesterday. The accumulation of water in various places was purely due to the inability of the sewers to discharge the water. Therefore, around 11:00 PM, the water gradually receded. Otherwise, the water accumulation would have been even higher, and the water would not have receded so quickly. The following are the details of the situation at that time, as investigated by reporters from this newspaper:

Water Floods Steps of Three Companies 119

Last night, during the heavy downpour, reporters from this newspaper traveled by car to various roads for inspection. The Bund area was relatively high, and it was low tide, so the roads were not flooded. The water accumulation in front of the Public Works Department on Fourth Road was five or six inches. The same was true for Zhejiang Road, Guangxi Road, and other places. The water at the entrance of the Tianchan Theater reached the stone steps, making it very inconvenient for audience members to enter the theater, so business was slow. The situation was similar on Second Road and Third Road. The entrance of the Grand Theater was higher, so it was not flooded, and the audience members were still crowded, with both upper and lower levels fully occupied. The water around the Three Companies area on Nanjing Road had flooded the steps. A few more inches, and there would be a risk of water damage to the large glass window advertisements. The construction site of the former Tianchan Theater had become a vast expanse of water, turning into a large pond. People waded through the water in various flooded areas of the roads, and cars were like ships, with water splashing everywhere. Good-natured teenagers and mischievous children held umbrellas and went barefoot, chasing each other in the water, which was very lively.

Route Six Trolleybuses Temporarily Suspended 120

The water depth near the intersection of Baoshan Road and Jielu Road, and the intersection of Laobazi Road and North Sichuan Road was about a foot deep. The Route Six circular trolleybuses were forced to suspend operations due to the flooding of the tracks. Small cars were also unable to start. Public buses and Route One and Two trolleybuses risked driving, driving very slowly in deep water. Rickshaws took advantage of the scarcity of transportation and charged exorbitant prices. The areas at the end of North Sichuan Road, such as Shigaota Road, had also become a swamp. Various dance halls and food shops near North Sichuan Road had sparse customers and were virtually closed. The French Concession and Nanshi areas were relatively high, so there was less water accumulation.

Water Accumulation at the Intersection of Zhejiang Road and Nanjing Road (Photo by Qichang) 121

Various Companies Strictly Prevent Water Damage 122

The Huangpu Bund and nearby Zhongchuan Road, Jiangxi Road, Yuanmingyuan Road, Museum, and other banks and companies took extra precautions against water damage because yesterday was Saturday and today would be a day off. For example, those with lower-level offices added hollow iron pillars to both sides of the windows and layered thick wooden boards within the iron pillars, filling the gaps with putty or lime so that they could be removed when they returned to work on Monday. Those without lower-level offices completely blocked the gaps under the floor with putty to allow air circulation. Temporary sandbag piles were everywhere. The Shanghai Telephone Company and others completely blocked the windows with putty, even though they had lower-level offices, in order to protect the machinery.

Situation in Various Places in Zhabei 123

Reporters went to various places in Zhabei for inspection last night. Arriving at Guangfu Road, they saw that the tide in the Suzhou River had risen greatly. The river water was level with the bank in the low-lying areas from the New Garbage Bridge to the New Big Bridge. The ships in the river appeared to be docked on the shore. At that time, there was a heavy downpour and thunder. When they arrived at the entrance of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau on Changan Road, the water accumulation in the middle of the road formed a river because it could not be discharged in time. Shops and homes used signboards and door panels to cross the water. Then, they passed through Huasheng Road and Datong Road to the Sun Temple Railway Crossing. The wasteland there had turned into a vast expanse of water. The fields on both sides of the Zhongxing Road Quanwan Guild Hall and the Republican New Road had also become a swamp. The terrain on the Zhongxing Road and other roads was higher, so it was clear at a glance, with few pedestrians. The area around the back of the Yong'an Company warehouse and the front, back, left, and right sides of the Xijin Guild Hall B House had also become a river. Heading south through Yongxing Road and Qiujiang Road to the north end of the Han Bridge, the water accumulation there was very deep.

Wall Collapse Injures Coppersmith 124

Near the Zhoujiazui Road of Hongkou Xinjiabang Road, the Jinchang Machinery Factory's back wall collapsed suddenly at around 6:30 PM yesterday, during the heavy downpour, crushing a room in the flat. A coppersmith named Zhu Jinhua, a native of Ningbo, aged 26, was crushed in the chest, the pressure very heavy. He was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by ambulance.

Comparison of Rainfall 125

The continuous autumn rain in this port has brought the temperature down to within 80 degrees. Bedding is needed for sleeping at night. However, the rainfall is still not comparable to the average amount in previous years. According to the Observatory yesterday, rainfall began in this port on the 11th, with a rainfall of 8 millimeters. On the 12th, it was 21.9 millimeters, on the 13th, 10.8 millimeters, and on the 14th, 7.1 millimeters. There was no report on yesterday's heavy rain. From January 1st to the evening of the 14th of this year, the total rainfall was 555.7 millimeters, which is more than half the average annual rainfall of 933.3 millimeters. Moreover, most of the rain each year falls in July. Now that it is after September, it is difficult to predict whether the rain will continue to fall to this half.

Overview of the Ministry of Finance's Implementation of the Abolition of Exorbitant and Miscellaneous Taxes 126

The Committee for the Consolidation of Local Taxes Compiles Implementation Report

Provinces Prepare Local Budgets and Report on Land

Regarding the abolition of exorbitant and miscellaneous taxes in all provinces and cities across the country, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi stated when he met with reporters from various newspapers the day before yesterday that progress had been made step by step and had achieved considerable results. He also stated that all implementation details had been successively announced by the Ministry of Finance's Committee for the Consolidation of Local Taxes. It has been learned that the committee has now compiled the third implementation report, which contains detailed reports on the abolition of exorbitant and miscellaneous taxes and the determination of local budgets in various provinces and cities. The reporter from New News Agency has extracted the main points as follows:

Determining Local Budgets 127

Consolidating local finances should be based on the determination of local budgets. The budgets for the 23rd year of the Republic for the counties in Jiangsu Province have largely been determined. Zhejiang Province has also convened county heads in groups to review and approve the estimated budgets for each county. Shaanxi, Hubei, and other provinces are convening county head meetings to prepare county budgets, which is also a major topic of discussion. Shanxi Province has approved the budgets for each county for this year, reducing them by more than 6 million yuan. Chahar Province has formulated 16 articles for handling local budgets in each county, which are based on the Ministry's regulations for handling county and city local budgets and key points. The Ministry is reviewing and forwarding them for implementation.

Unifying Tax Collection Agencies 128

Consolidating local tax collection should focus on unified collection and disbursement. Henan Province has established a unified collection office for business tax and slaughter tax. Anhui Province is planning to establish a local tax bureau. Jiangsu Province has established miscellaneous tax collection offices in various counties. Fujian Province is also considering selecting locations to establish county finance bureaus. Although these measures still require careful discussion and gradual implementation, this reform will make it easier to comprehensively review tax collection. All system improvements and personnel training will be easier to centralize.

Handling Land Reporting 129

Regarding the land reporting case, Zhejiang Province has requested to continue handling land survey and consolidation of map registers by region. Jiangxi Province has requested information on the ongoing aerial survey. The Ministry has responded to both, following the provisions of Article 25 of the outline promulgated by the Executive Yuan, and instructed them to investigate and handle the matters separately. If they do not comply with the previous regulations, they should expedite the reporting. The four counties of Yixing, Jiangsu Province, have already begun handling the reporting and have completed it ahead of schedule. On September 1st, a meeting was convened with the county heads of Jiangdu, Taicang, Tongshan, and other counties to thoroughly comply with the outline promulgated by the Central Government and continue handling the reporting. The committee dispatched experts to attend the meeting. According to reports, Anhui and Henan provinces have either established reporting offices or are consulting with provincial land administration agencies to plan in detail. Hebei and Shaanxi provinces will also carefully plan the implementation at the administrative group meetings.

Abolishing Exorbitant Taxes and Reducing Surcharges 130

Several provinces and cities have reported the abolition of exorbitant taxes and the reduction of surcharges. The matters related to local compensation have been handled by the local authorities. As for the matters related to the central government, such as tobacco and alcohol license taxes, since July 1st, when the responsibility for handling them was transferred to the local authorities, various cities have reported that they have taken over and consolidated them, and tax revenues are very buoyant. The Ministry has now dispatched personnel to conduct on-site investigations to determine whether the abolished items have been genuinely stopped and whether the compensation funds have been properly allocated. The central government will base its policy of approving and allocating compensation funds on the results of the on-site investigations and the extent of local efforts.

It sent a telegram to the Executive Committee of the Central Party Headquarters, stating, "To the Nanjing Chinese Kuomintang Central Executive Committee, since the September 18th Incident, the national crisis has become increasingly urgent, and the people are suffering. Looking ahead, we feel even more heartache. Our party bears a major mission and must unite sincerely to overcome the difficulties together. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Issues Declaration Yesterday for UN Non-Permanent Council 133

Since Turkey is Competing as a European Country,

Then Asia Should Give China a Chance for Re-election

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued a declaration regarding the re-election of non-permanent council members of the UN Council of Ministers, stating: At this session of the re-election of non-permanent council members of the International League of Nations Executive Council, our country's representative Guo Luojin has detailed the importance of China's position in the international arena and the faithful sacrifices it has made for the League of Nations over the years, expressing that friendly countries should give China another chance to be elected, so that it can do its utmost. We believe that these claims are fair and reasonable and represent the unanimous demands of the people. Now, in the capacity of citizens, our association still wishes to make some statements. The League of Nations is an organization of universal nature, so it is an immutable principle to fairly distribute its representatives according to region. Since 1926, when the Executive Council members adopted the system of distribution by continent, Asia has occupied two seats, Europe has occupied eight seats, and the Americas have occupied four seats for permanent and non-permanent council members. Although it is not stipulated in the Covenant, it has become the unwritten constitution of the League of Nations. Turkey is China's oldest friend and its newest friend. We deeply admire and are very hopeful that it can become a pillar of the League of Nations and make efforts for it. However, Turkey, due to its historical and diplomatic relations, is really centered in Europe. Therefore, in its petition this time, it frankly stated that it considers itself a European country, just like the Russians whose land spans Europe and Asia, and all countries recognize it as a European country. Now that Japan has already withdrawn from the League, if there is another change in the seat of non-permanent council members, then Asia, which has the largest area and the largest population in the world, will not be able to participate in the organization of the Executive Council. This is indeed an unprecedented change since the founding of the League of Nations and is greatly contrary to the principle of universality and fairness. This is not only regrettable for the Asian countries but also regrettable for all the member states of the League of Nations. We therefore earnestly hope that all member states of the League of Nations will maintain the system of distribution of League of Nations council members by continent and give China a chance for re-election.

Minister of Finance Kong Denies Borrowing to Purchase Military Supplies 134

Cotton and Wheat Loans are Used Entirely for Production and Construction

12.5 Million Yuan Has Been Used

According to Xin Xin News Agency, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi denied yesterday the report by the Washington Congressional Committee Investigating International Arms Trade that cotton and wheat loans were used to purchase military supplies, saying that when the Chinese government signed the cotton and wheat loan agreement, the Central Political Conference decided to use it for China's production and construction. To date, 12.5 million yuan has been used, and its uses are as follows: 8.4 million yuan for the National Economic Committee to engage in construction, 3.8 million yuan for the recovery of bandit areas, and 300,000 yuan for disaster relief in Sichuan. The remaining funds have not been used. Kong also said that the National Economic Committee has also resolved to use cotton and wheat loans for production and construction, designating them for the construction of highways, improvement of hygiene, improvement of Chinese silk, relief of Chinese yarn, tea, fuel, and construction in Jiangxi and the Northwest. According to a Washington AP dispatch, US Congressional International Arms Trade Investigation Committee Chairman Mr. Nye announced that when China successfully negotiated a large cotton and wheat loan with the United States in 1932, China exchanged some cotton and wheat for military supplies from Italy. Kong's above remarks were probably made in reference to this.

Petition Representatives of Overseas Chinese Expelled from Japan Return to Shanghai 135

Ministry of Foreign Affairs Promises to Continue Serious Negotiations

Overseas Chinese who were expelled and repatriated from Japan, in batches arriving in Shanghai, specially elected representatives Chen Fengqing, Xia Yongchang, Yang Zhanhong, and three others to go to Beijing to petition the central government and report the process. Chen Fengqing and the three have returned to Shanghai at 7:00 AM yesterday. The reporter from New News Agency specially went to inquire about the process of petitioning, and the details are as follows:

Process of Petitioning 136

According to Chen Fengqing, after we arrived in Beijing, we first went to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to petition. Chairman Chen personally received us, explained the association's relief plan for overseas Chinese, and gave us 15 yuan each for travel expenses. Then we petitioned the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, since the Japanese expulsion of overseas Chinese occurred, it has repeatedly made representations to the Japanese side. Now, it will continue to conduct serious negotiations. All the expelled overseas Chinese deeply hope that the government will negotiate with the Japanese side to have the confiscated property returned. Chen also stated that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission have both made instructions and passed them on to all overseas Chinese for their information.

Instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 137

Informed, the Ministry is very concerned about the plight of the overseas Chinese. Since this matter occurred, the Ministry has repeatedly made representations to the Japanese side in the case. According to the previous situation, we will continue to conduct serious negotiations to achieve results. As for the representative's face-to-face request to find work and seek relief, we have transferred the matter to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for handling. This is hereby notified for information, these instructions.

Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission Reply 138

Received and noted. This commission is deeply concerned about the expulsion of our overseas Chinese by Japan and the confiscation of their property. In addition to sending a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs instructing the ambassador to Japan to lodge a strong protest, the 78th Standing Committee meeting of this commission has resolved that each returned overseas Chinese refugee from Japan will be given a subsidy of five yuan. Instructions have been issued to our personnel stationed in Shanghai to implement this decision. Regarding fundamental relief, this commission is currently purchasing farmland in Xuancheng County, Anhui Province, to build a "Qiaole Village" (Overseas Chinese Happiness Village) to resettle unemployed overseas Chinese. When the time comes for its establishment, separate notifications will be issued. Please take note.

### Two Exchanges Merged Yesterday 140

Employees of the Merchandise Exchange Dismissed with One Year's Salary

Gold Exchange to Hold Shareholders Meeting This Afternoon

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the long-brewing merger between the gold department of the Merchandise Exchange and the Gold Exchange was implemented yesterday. The Merchandise Exchange was established on July 1, 1920 (Year 9 of the Republic), and has been in operation for 14 years. It dealt with a wide variety of commodities, including securities, gold, cotton yarn, grains, and hides, hence the comprehensive name "Merchandise." Later, the exchange was affected by the global economic depression, leading to a decline in business. Therefore, the "Merchandise" designation was cancelled, and part of the margin fund was merged with the Gold Exchange. It is reported that, in terms of the merger, the Merchandise Exchange, besides 25 brokers who were incorporated into the Gold Exchange through a lottery, the majority of the brokers were dismissed. As a result, many brokers have been switching professions or closing early in recent days. Regarding the rumor that the Merchandise Exchange staff would join the Gold Exchange to gain experience, this is not true. All employees of the Merchandise Exchange have been dismissed. Leaders such as directors and chairmen have also sought their own livelihoods. However, the members of the council, considering the hard work of the employees, trainees, and servants for over a decade, have granted each of them one year's salary as severance pay. It is also heard that the Gold Exchange has decided to convene an extraordinary shareholders' meeting this afternoon (Sunday) at 2:00 PM at the market to discuss important matters such as the conclusion of the merger, ratification of the contract, amendment of the articles of association, and increase in capital.

### Municipal Chamber of Commerce Appeals to Ministry of Finance to Revise Ink Tax Assessment 144

Must Conform to Ink Merchants' Selling Prices as the Standard

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of submitting a petition: On the 14th of this month, we received a letter from the Ink and Brush Industry Association stating, 'Our association's ink industry originated in the Southern Tang Dynasty and was originally based in Huizhou. Since the opening of maritime trade, most have relocated from Huizhou to Shanghai to establish factories for manufacturing, to supply the needs of the entire country. In the late Qing Dynasty, ink and brushes were considered important tools for promoting culture. Aside from taxes on raw materials, donation and tax registers specifically designated ink and brushes for special tax-exempt treatment. The ink tax began in 1913 (Year 2 of the Republic). At that time, the price of ink was 50 to 60 taels of silver per 100 catties, but customs assessed the value at 80 taels for taxation. Merchants accepted this reluctantly during the warlord period. Later, when the price of ink fell to 40 taels per 100 catties, the tax rate was still levied based on 80 taels, an injustice beyond compare. In recent years, with the abolition of the tael and the adoption of the yuan, the price of ink is only 50 to 60 yuan. When reporting taxes, customs sometimes used 60 yuan as the tax rate, and sometimes calculated based on 80 taels, resulting in inconsistent tariffs that disrupted the business. This has a significant impact on operations. Furthermore, in the four northeastern provinces and Korea, Japan has increased tax rates, creating obstacles. Since domestic exports cannot be preferentially exempted from taxes to provide assistance, how can we excessively high prices and heavy taxes to destroy the livelihood of ink merchants? Therefore, we specifically request that your esteemed chamber forward this matter to the Shanghai Customs Office, stating that the export tax on ink must conform to the selling price of the ink merchants, or else the assessment should not exceed 60 yuan per 100 catties, so that the declining ink industry may have a chance to survive.' After reviewing the information, it is reasonable to request that the Ministry review the situation. Since the revision of the tariff regulations, the export of national ink has changed from 7.05% of the value to 5%. In principle, ink merchants seem to have reduced their burden, but because the price of ink has decreased while customs assessments remain the same, the actual tax burden on merchants has increased. Although Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Export Taxes states that exporters who are dissatisfied with the prices set by customs may protest to the Customs Commissioner within 20 days, according to the situation described in the association's letter, the overvaluation is not accidental but occurs almost every time. Ink merchants cannot be compared to government agencies or other organizations and do not have personnel dedicated to writing official documents. They mostly endure in silence. Therefore, this relief measure cannot be widely effective. Based on the information presented above, it is appropriate to request that the Ministry review and approve an order to the Customs Office to mediate the current prices and revise the assessment to avoid excessive harassment. This would be in the public interest."

### "Shen Bao Monthly" September Issue Published 149
