### Navigation Cooperation Plan Drafted 151

Submitted to the Ministry of Communications for Review

According to the Central News Agency, the Navigation Design Committee, jointly established by the Shanghai Shipping Association and the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was ordered by the Ministry of Communications to draft a navigation cooperation plan to reduce competition among industry players and strengthen shipping capabilities. Since its establishment in mid-April, the committee has agreed on the basic principles of the plan and tasked a specially formed expert committee with drafting the plan. The Ministry of Communications has also dispatched Gao Tingzi, Director of the Shipping Administration Department, and Director Peng Hu to attend as on-site representatives. It is reported that the cooperation plan drafted by the committee has been completed after five months of research and discussion. The plan was approved at an extraordinary plenary committee meeting this past Tuesday (the 21st) and will soon be submitted to the Ministry for approval. Peng Hu has also submitted a report to the Ministry on the details of his attendance at the meetings. The Design Committee's work is now complete, and it is awaiting instructions from the Ministry on whether to continue its existence.

### Difficulty in Establishing Maritime Court 152

According to the Central News Agency, after the Executive Yuan approved the establishment of the Maritime Dispute Resolution Committee under the jurisdiction of the Shipping Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, the Shanghai Shipping Association argued that the committee's functions were limited to mediation and arbitration, similar to the existing Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee. Therefore, the association strongly advocated to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry the establishment of a maritime court to specifically adjudicate ship-related cases. According to information obtained by reporters from the Shipping Administration Bureau, the establishment of a maritime court is very difficult and may not be approved for some time. Although the Maritime Dispute Resolution Committee is similar in nature to the Collision Committee, its scope is broader. In addition to ship collision disputes, all maritime disputes can be accepted. Compared to the existing setup, it is more complete. Once the committee is established, the Collision Committee may be abolished.

### Investigation of Disaster Situation in the Fourth District of Liyang 153

This year's drought has been most severe in Liyang County in Jiangsu Province. Among the six districts of Liyang, the fourth district is the most severely affected. In order to seek immediate relief, the people of the district organized a begging group and appointed representatives Rui Mengzhou, Tang Xiuzhang, Chen Hongcai, Shi Jiagen, and Shi Jincheng to go to the Wuxi-Shanghai area to appeal to philanthropists. They also sent letters detailing the disaster situation. Charity groups in Wuxi and Shanghai have now appointed Li Juncikai, Shi Junxiangchen, Xu Junyili, and Li Junzongyuan to visit the district on the 10th of this month. When District Chief Rui Baoyuan heard that the committee members would arrive at Nanduzhen by car from Liyang City, he hired a small car and sent personnel to meet them. After arriving at Nanduzhen, Li Jun and the others rested briefly and switched to small cars to travel through Qiangbu and other places. Along the way, they saw continuous stretches of white fields and withered seedlings, causing them to sigh. In Qiangbuzhen, they saw a man named Ji Shan from Jiangbei who, due to starvation, had committed suicide by hanging. Feeling compassion, they immediately provided 12 yuan for the cost of a coffin. Along the way, old people, women, and children begged for food in endless streams. Li Jun and the others gave out corner tickets or silver dollars as requested. Even if they were not begging but were determined to be genuinely poor, they gave what they could to ensure that no one was left empty-handed. At 2:00 PM, they arrived at the town where District Chief Rui and Police Chief Qiu, along with the town chiefs and business leaders, were waiting to welcome them. After Li Jun and the others got out of the car, they were led by the District Chief to the District Office for a warm reception. In the evening, the District Chief invited the committee members to a discussion meeting at the District Office. Attendees included representatives from the begging group, town chiefs, and Qiu, Chief of the Public Security Bureau in the town, as well as Tang, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce. Li Jun and the others advocated setting up factories to provide porridge, so that every drop of benefit could reach the disaster victims. They agreed to set up four porridge factories (Shangpeibu, Shangxingbu, Tangjiaqiao, and Qiangbu). After the meeting, the clock struck eleven, and they retired to the District Office. The next morning, accompanied by representatives of the begging group, they went to Dongba to purchase relief rice. It is said that they still needed to go to Liyang City to attend a banquet hosted by County Magistrate Chen to discuss matters further. Li Jun and the others can be described as generous and tireless.

### Shipping Administration Bureau Investigates the Bao Hua Ship Incident 154

The Ping An Company's Bao Hua ship ran aground outside Sanhe Port, causing the ship to list sideways on the sea. Passengers on board were unable to escape from the cabins, resulting in dozens drowning in the sea. The ship's stewards and laborers also fell into the sea and died, and their bodies have not yet been recovered. Afterwards, the shipowners reported to the company that everyone was busy trying to save the ship and that they did not know the exact number of people who fell into the sea. However, according to people on the ship, no more than four passengers drowned. Only one of the passengers who fell into the sea was able to cling to an empty bamboo basket thrown overboard by the ship. The waves carried him to Yonglong Port, where he was fortunate to be able to swim and save his life. However, he had drifted 16 miles out to sea. It is unknown what happened to those who could not swim. It is said that most of the people who fell into the water were hardworking people from Sanhe Port and Niutou Port who were disembarking. After receiving the company's report, the Shipping Administration Bureau determined that the incident involved a commercial ship and decided to launch a thorough investigation. They will strictly investigate the cause of the Bao Hua ship's grounding, whether it could have been avoided, and the total number of passengers who died on the spot. It is necessary to emphasize the importance of human life. As for the cargo that was thrown overboard during the emergency and the loss due to water damage in the ship's cabins, the company has notified the cargo owners. Yesterday, the Ping An Company ordered the Bao Hua ship to resume its normal route to Chongming. It is not yet known whether the company will provide compensation to the family of the deceased steward Liu Zichang and the workers. Furthermore, the ship's purser is named Dong Chunfang. Yesterday's report stating that Li Yaoting was the company's general manager was incorrect.

The Cai Yangqi Case Awaits Resolution Through Foreign Negotiations 161

The First Special Court Held Another Hearing Yesterday

Defendant Lang Zuyin Still Refuses to Appear

The Shanghai First Special District Court accepted a case during the summer involving Lang Zuyin, a Chinese detective of the Lao Zha Police Station, who was accused of using electric shock to injure Cai Yangqi. The court held nearly ten hearings, but because the defendant Lang Zuyin did not accept the summons and refused to appear in court for interrogation, the trial could not begin. Three months have passed, and the case remains unresolved. This is the first thorny case handled since our country recovered legal rights in the Shanghai concession and established a formal court. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, another hearing was scheduled for the case. The presiding judge, Liu Yugui, followed the usual procedure and issued a summons in advance, ordering the bailiffs to deliver it to both the plaintiff and the defendant. However, when the hearing time arrived, the defendant Lang Zuyin still did not surrender. The situation was no different from previous hearings. Cai Yangqi sat in the waiting seat, and another defendant, Bao Defu, was also present. Since the plaintiff was Cai Yangqi's wife, Judge Liu summoned Cai's wife to the plaintiff's stand and informed her that the case had been submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for negotiation with the relevant country's ambassador, but there were no results so far. Therefore, the trial could not proceed. Once the issue was resolved, another hearing would be scheduled, and a summons would be issued. The woman heard the notification and left with her husband. Bao Defu and the lawyers representing the case also left their seats. Therefore, when the case can proceed smoothly depends on the results of negotiations in Beijing.

Two Railway Bureaus Decide to Build Their Own Building 163

Recovering the Shengshunli Property

Construction Cost of 700,000 Yuan

According to the Central News Agency, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus have decided to build their own building because the rent paid for office space is too high. The Ministry of Railways has approved the plan, and the architectural drawings have been drafted. The construction cost is 700,000 yuan, which will be allocated from the employee welfare fund. The construction site is selected at the eastern end of the North Railway Station, where the Shengshunli buildings will be demolished and rebuilt. According to sources from the Railway Bureau, the site covers more than 20 mu and is the Railway Bureau's property. Twenty years ago, it was leased to the gentry and merchant Yu Qiaqing for the construction of buildings. At that time, a contract was signed for a lease term of 30 years. Upon expiration, all surface buildings would be returned to the Railway Bureau at no cost. If the Railway Bureau needed to recover the land for its own use after 20 years, it could recover the surface buildings at an assessed value. By the end of this year, the 20-year term has expired, and the Railway Bureau needs to recover the land to build its own building. Therefore, it has contacted Yu, who demanded 400,000 yuan in compensation. The Bureau believes the asking price is too high, so it is negotiating. However, the Bureau's plan to recover the land for construction will not change.

Record of the Trial of Two Escaped Convicts 165

The Two Convicts Claimed to Have Been Abused and Beaten After the Escape

After Speaking, They Took Off Their Clothes to Show Scars, Crying Bitterly

Guard Fu Maoshun's Residence is Restricted, Temporarily Staying in Prison

The Second Special District Prison on Masnan Road in the French Concession had an incident on the morning of the 9th of this month at around 3:00 AM. When the inmates of each cell were opened, nine-four-zero, a serious criminal, Zhang Weicai, nine-nine-two, Zhao Yunzu, and Liu Agui, a petty thief, attempted to escape. Zhang and Zhao forced Liu to climb the wall with a rope to escape, but Liu panicked and fell halfway down, injuring the back of his head. He was sent to Guangci Hospital, but died the following evening due to the severity of his injuries. The warden ordered Zhang and Zhao to be fitted with heavy shackles and await investigation and prosecution. This has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that the rope used by the convicts to escape was made by tearing strips from their clothes and trousers. The warden, Sun Xiong, has prepared a document to transfer the two convicts, Zhang and Zhao, and the witness, thief Xia Ajin, as well as the evidence, rope, torn cloth strips, and two long bench boards, to the Procuratorate of the Second Special Court for investigation and prosecution. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Prosecutor Wang Ren and Clerk Zhao Yifen specially opened the Sixth Tribunal for investigation and ordered the two convicts and Xia to be brought in for interrogation. The prison also sent the guards who discovered the incident at the time, Xiao Wenyin, Nie Zhenchun, and Fu Maoshun, to the court as witnesses. According to Zhang and Zhao, they admitted that they colluded with the deceased Liu Agui to escape. It started with jokes, and they first made ropes from their clothes, trousers, and socks, and then secretly filed off their shackles. When they saw Liu fall and get injured, they were afraid to escape. The official summoned the witness Xia Ajin, who testified, "That day, I saw Zhang and Zhao walking out of the room, and I immediately reported to the guard Fu Maoshun, but Fu did not care. Later, the second time I saw a dark shadow on the wall, I went to report to Fu, but Fu still ignored me." According to the guards Xiao Wenyin, Nie Zhenchun, and Fu Maoshun, they testified about the circumstances of the discovery at the time. However, Fu testified that Xia did not report any incident to him beforehand. By this point, it was noon. The official ordered Zhang and Zhao and Xia Ajin to be sent back to prison for custody, and Xiao and Nie were ordered to return. Fu Maoshun's residence was restricted, and he was temporarily detained in prison, not allowed to leave. After the announcement, Zhang claimed that he had confidential information to report to the court and requested that the guards in the court be dismissed. The official granted the request and ordered the guards to withdraw. Zhang claimed that because they failed to escape, they were fitted with heavy shackles, handcuffed, and beaten by guards and officials, including one named Huang Baochang, who pinned me to the ground and beat me with fists and feet, causing serious injuries. I shouted for help, and the inmates in the prison responded. I was dragged outside and beaten, with 30 blows every hour, for a total of three days and nights, lasting 53 hours. After Liu Agui fell and got injured, not only was he not sent to the hospital for treatment, but he was also tied up and beaten in the same way, which led to his death. Zhao Yunzu's testimony was the same as Zhang's. The two convicts were tearful when they spoke and took off their clothes to request an examination of the scars and asked for permission to accuse them of assault. They also expressed their unwillingness to return to prison, fearing further torture. The official ordered the bailiffs to send the two convicts to the forensic doctor for examination. At the same time, he summoned Xiao, Nie, and Fu, the three guards, who all claimed to be unaware of the beatings. The court then adjourned the hearing and announced that it would be reconvened at a later date for further verification.

5,000 yuan to redeem us. Now, we think that such extortion should be a crime, so we escaped." After District Chief Wang received the confession, he ordered the original detectives to arrest Wang Xiaosizi. Qin Da, Wang Chengji, Zhou Jiahe, and Huang Baofu are still being closely investigated.

Fudian New Bank Asks for Severe Punishment of Counterfeiters 166

The Main Culprit, Li Yunchang, Was Arrested in Yunnan for Manufacturing Counterfeit Money

After Being Released on Amnesty, He Sneaked into Shanghai and Dared to Resume His Old Business

According to the Shenshi News Agency's local report, the Special Agency Inspector of the French Concession Police Department, Jin Jiulin, and others seized a large number of counterfeit Fudian New Bank banknotes at the intersection of Baylor Road and Father Lao Road the night before and arrested the manufacturers Li Yunchang, Liu Guangsheng, Ji Jinquan, and others and escorted them to the police station. This morning, they were transferred to the Second Special Court for trial. The police department is still investigating. The Shenshi News Agency reporter interviewed Dong Sixun, the business director of Fudian New Bank, about this matter yesterday. He agreed to an interview and stated that the bank was very angry about this incident. The main culprit in the counterfeiting, Li Yunchang, had repeatedly manufactured counterfeit money in Yunnan and was arrested and imprisoned by the police authorities. After being released on amnesty, he sneaked into Shanghai and resumed his old tricks, manufacturing counterfeit money. Fortunately, he was caught, which shows that justice will always prevail. Dong also said that the bank does not issue banknotes, and the counterfeit money is mostly subsidiary coins, which have little impact on the bank. However, the culprit dared to profit by impersonation, endangering the public, which is hateful. The bank will send a letter to the Second Special Court through its agent lawyer, requesting severe punishment.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Investigates the Yadong Night Market Agency 167

Discovers Many Gold and Silver Goods Trading Markets

Reports to the Social Affairs Bureau to Be Submitted to the Ministry of Industry for Approval

The Yadong Gold and Silver Goods Night Market Agency at 989 Avenue Joffre, Shanghai, was founded by the American V. M. Haimoriech and began operations on May 7th of this year. It buys and sells gold bars, cotton, wheat, rubber, silver, and other goods for customers at the exchange and charges commissions. Because it violated Articles 10, Paragraph 1, and 16 of the Exchange Law, the Ministry of Industry instructed the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau to ban it, ordering it to remove all signs and advertisements in front of the store by September 10th of this year. Later, because the agency moved to another location without a fixed address, the instructions could not be delivered. The Social Affairs Bureau ordered the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to inquire and forward the instructions and assigned staff to investigate whether it had been complied with every night before September 10th and report back for verification. This has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent staff members Dong Wenzhong and Xue Jianxin to investigate various exchanges. They have completed their investigation and prepared a report, which has been approved by the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and reported to the Social Affairs Bureau to be submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. According to the findings obtained by the Xinsheng News Agency, they are recorded as follows:

Cessation of Operations 168

The Yadong Gold and Silver Goods Night Market Agency V. M. Haimoriech Co. on Avenue Joffre has indeed ceased operations. It ceased operations and moved to another location in July. The signs and advertisements in front of the store have also been removed. The owner of the agency, Haimoriech, is currently working as a jockey for the Chinese Ma Xiangsheng and also works part-time in the bidding business at the China Exchange Company on Central Road.

Other Discoveries 169

However, according to the investigation results, many gold and silver goods trading markets similar to exchanges have been established in this city. There are China and Central Exchange Companies on Central Road. At 55 Haining Road, there is the Shanghai Bidding Company. Customers only need to pay a deposit of 10 yuan per lot to trade, and one or two lots can also be traded, providing customers with the convenience of small investments. At 15 Xinkang Road, there is a night market bidding trading market with the English words "Asiatic Gold Stock Exchange" written on the glass window and the Chinese sign "Baodayong Gold Store" written next to the wall at the entrance.

Organizational Situation 170

The night market is jointly operated by seven Chinese and foreign merchants. Among the shareholders, there are former employees of the Yadong Night Market Agency. It is said that Ma Weiqu has no involvement. The staff is small, but the internal layout is clean and tidy, with price boards for gold, silver, and other goods. Baodayong Gold Store was founded by Mr. Xu, a broker No. 23 of the Shanghai Securities and Goods Exchange, and is the manager of the market.

Business Nature 171

The business hours are set from 10:00 PM to 1:00 AM every night. Since operations began on August 6th, 30 to 40 lots of bidding transactions have been concluded every night. Its business is to buy and sell bidding gold, silver, cotton, wheat, rubber, and other goods for customers at the exchange with brokers or members of the Yadong Night Gold Industry Exchange for the purpose of differential trading and charge high commissions. A goods and gold and silver trading market has been established, translated as "Asian Gold Industry Exchange." However, it is not possible to determine whether it is a disguised organization of the Yadong Night Market Agency or whether it is still managed by Haimoriech. The staff of the market is tight-lipped about the investigators, so it is not possible to obtain accurate evidence of the Yadong Night Market Agency, and the instructions cannot be delivered.

Violation of Laws 172

In summary, the above-mentioned trading markets actually violate Article 2 of the Exchange Law, "An exchange for the trading of securities or similar goods. Only one may be established in each area," Article 16, "No one may operate as an agent, introducer, or transmitter of exchange trading commissions, except for brokers or members who have been approved," and Article 40, "No one may establish a market similar to an exchange outside of the exchange for the purpose of differential trading and conduct trading." How should these be dealt with? A report has been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for review.

Page 13

Zhang Gongquan Returns to Shanghai from Jiangxi for Inspection 173

Talks About Helping Jiangxi's Declining Porcelain Industry

According to the Shenshi News Agency, Zhang Gongquan, General Manager of the Bank of China, went to North China to inspect the economic and financial situation and then went down the Yangtze River to Jiangxi to visit Chiang Kai-shek and inspect the current situation of the porcelain industry in Jiangxi Province. Zhang has now transferred from Xun to Beijing and returned to Shanghai by train. The Shenshi News Agency reporter paid a special visit yesterday to inquire about everything. The details are recorded as follows:

Inspection of the Economy of North China 174

Zhang Gongquan set off from Shanghai by ship last month to understand the financial situation in various places and went to North China, Tianjin, and other places for inspection. He held talks with leaders of the financial and business circles in various places and made detailed observations on the economic decline and other realities. Then, he took a train south from Tianjin and went to Jiangxi after arriving in Beijing, inspecting the commercial and production situation in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River along the way. He also went to Lu Mountain at Chiang's invitation to discuss important issues such as the current financial and economic situation with Finance Minister Kong and others. During his stay in Jiangxi, he also inspected the province's porcelain industry and the rural economy. He has now finished his work and returned to Shanghai. According to Zhang, the impressions he gained from this inspection were very good.

Decline of Jiangxi's Porcelain Industry 175

Zhang told the Shenshi News Agency reporter yesterday about his inspection of the porcelain industry in Jiangxi: "I paid attention to the porcelain industry in Jiangxi during my trip. Due to various reasons, the porcelain industry in the province has recently entered a state of extreme decline. The main reason is that the makers of porcelain blanks, the kiln operators, and the suppliers of raw materials do not cooperate with each other, which has created the main internal factor of its decline. In places such as Jingdezhen and other famous porcelain producing areas, the makers of blanks are mostly small businesses with capital of no more than two or three hundred yuan. They have not received porcelain industry education, have no artistic knowledge, and have not studied market needs. They also do not know how to use scientific methods. The kiln operators have also been affected by the pressure of foreign goods on the porcelain industry in recent years, which has led to a decline in business. The customers who entrust them to fire porcelain are decreasing, so they have to be held hostage by those who entrust them to fire. They only open the kiln when it is full, so the makers of porcelain blanks have to wait for a long time before they can get their goods, and they cannot meet the needs of the market quickly.

Increased Production Costs 176

Furthermore, the kiln owners only know how to reduce fuel and try to increase the height of the kiln as much as possible in order to collect more porcelain blanks and make more profit. As a result, the fired porcelain blanks are easily damaged and of poor quality. The kiln owners not only do not compensate for the damage but also do not refund the firing fee to those who entrusted them to fire the porcelain blanks. On average, 40 pieces of goods must be prepared for every 100 pieces to compensate for damage. As a result, the cost increases, and the price of the goods naturally increases. It is impossible to compete with scientific and low-priced foreign porcelain products, and they are gradually eliminated.

Bad Atmosphere Among Workers 177

Jiangxi Province is a region that produces porcelain raw materials. Most of the production in the region is controlled by local tyrants, who try to raise the value as much as possible. Therefore, porcelain blank makers cannot obtain raw materials at favorable prices to reduce the value of their goods. In addition, porcelain workers in Jiangxi Province lack discipline and training and are mostly wandering and unrestrained. The atmosphere is very bad, and work efficiency is also declining. The future of the entire Chinese porcelain industry is in crisis.

Future Improvement Measures 178

In order to improve the porcelain industry in Jiangxi, it is first necessary to have good local officials who thoroughly rectify the local atmosphere, correct the bad habits of the porcelain workers, and increase their productivity. At the same time, it is necessary to seek immediate solutions to the raw material prices and the control of kiln owners. In the active aspect, it is necessary to have specialized knowledge to train a new class of porcelain industry workers, improve the skills of kiln owners, and strive to promote reform. Only then can there be hope for the future. The Jiangxi Provincial authorities have hired Mr. Du Chongyuan to organize the Jiujiang Porcelain Industry Company. The Provincial Government has promised to allocate 200,000 yuan to promote it. Commercial shares will be given residual interest by the government. The improvement and relief of the porcelain industry in Jingdezhen has also been taken over by the National Economic Commission, which is responsible for allocating funds to help its development, so as to seek the revival of China's porcelain industry.

Japanese Red Pill Manufacturing Facility Raided on Doulean Road 179

Japanese Fled Upon Hearing the News, Leaving No Trace

Police Arrested Several Chinese

The Desvai Road Police Station suddenly received a notice from the Japanese Consulate at 4:30 PM yesterday, dispatching police to a Japanese residence at 59 Doulean Road at the end of North Sichuan Road, which was a red pill manufacturing facility. The police chief immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to rush to the scene to surround and arrest them. Upon reaching the destination, the Japanese at the address had fled upon hearing the news, leaving no trace. Only two or three Chinese were arrested, and several red pills and red pill manufacturing tools were seized and taken to the police station for investigation by the court. When the detectives arrived at the scene, a Ningbo man named Hong Xiuqing, 23 years old, was eager to escape and jumped from the third floor, breaking his back and losing consciousness. He was later spotted by the police and sent to Tongren Hospital in a car, then transferred to the police hospital for treatment.

Man and Woman Commit Suicide by Poison 180

Suicide Note States Cause as Economic Pressure

At a certain hotel at No. 200 Shansi Road, a man and a woman, each a traveler, arrived around 5:00 PM the night before and requested lodging. The hotel clerk led them to Room 520 on the fifth floor. The man was wearing a bluish-gray woolen single-layer shirt, and the woman wore a white cotton shirt and trousers. They paid the room fee of five yuan and signed the registration book as Zhao Jiaji, a local, 29 years old; the woman was his wife, 25 years old. As usual, the tea server brought tea and water and then left. Later in the evening, the man ordered two servings of coffee and chicken rice from the tea server to eat with the woman. After finishing their meal, they closed the door and went to sleep. However, at about 5:00 AM the next morning, the tea server suddenly heard the sound of a broken bowl coming from the room, followed by groans. Feeling suspicious, they quickly opened the door and entered, finding the man collapsed on a sofa chair and the woman lying across the bed. Both were pale and unconscious. On the table was an empty bottle of medicine. They urgently reported to the clerk, who in turn reported to the police station. The two were transported by car to Renji Hospital for treatment. The hospital examination revealed that they had both taken Lysol poison. Despite various attempts to resuscitate them, they ultimately succumbed to the poisoning and died around 5:30 AM. The police station was notified to send the corpses to the mortuary for examination. A suicide note and several business cards were found on their person, printed with "Zhang Jiaju, style Yimin, Shanghai Dacheng Coal Company, 76 Dapu Bridge, French Concession, telephone 75685 ext." Detectives immediately went to inquire at that address. It was reported that Zhang Jiaju, from Shaoxing, had indeed worked as a salesman for the coal company but had since left. As to whether the woman was Zhang's wife, they claimed not to know. The suicide note stated that they were suffering from economic pressure, but it was vague on details. The police station is still investigating the matter.

Strangled Male Body Found on Great Western Road 181

Clothes and Pants Not Completely Wet

Appears to be Body Moved After Death

Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, at the intersection of Great Western Road and Difeng Road in western Shanghai, Officer No. 2660 of the Jing'an Temple police station discovered the body of a man who had been strangled. The man was about 30 years old, of medium build, wearing a black cloth short shirt, white cloth trousers, black thread socks, a monk's haircut, and one shoe. His body was lying on the south side of the road. The police station was notified, and Detective Qian Xianting was ordered to investigate. He saw two ropes around the man's neck, one a brown rope and the other resembling a woman's belt. When the detectives arrived, it was still raining, but the man's clothes and pants were not completely wet. Therefore, it was suspected that the strangling occurred elsewhere and the body was moved to this location. The body was immediately sent to the Red Cross Hospital, but resuscitation efforts failed, and he died. The body was then transferred to the Filon Road mortuary. Around 10:00 AM, Tang, a prosecutor from the First Special Court, accompanied by forensic doctor Zhang Yan, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. After the detectives reported the results of their investigation, Prosecutor Tang declared that the unidentified man had indeed been strangled to death. While the police station investigates the perpetrator, the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.

Pi Bingzhang, a Chinese detective of the Huishan Police Station, learned that someone had privately set up a morphine injection den at No. 37 Yuanfang Lane, Broadway Road, to make illicit profits. He and a team of Chinese and Western police officers raided the location the day before yesterday and arrested eight people from Jiangbei, including Wang Er, Yang Gensheng, and Xie Jinshan. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated the facts and requested prosecution. The evidence was presented for inspection. Detective Pi Bingzhang then reported the circumstances of the arrest of each defendant. After Judge Wu Zehan interrogated the defendants, the court sentenced Wang Er and Yang Gensheng to 40 days of detention each, and Xie Jinshan, Wu Jinchun, Cao Jinxu, and Cai Hongliang to 20 days each as a warning. Ji Dexin and Min Zehong were found not guilty, and the evidence was confiscated. Lawyer Li waived appeal for Ji and Min, and they were immediately released.

Reading and Q&A

Attitude Towards Occupation 198

Answering Mr. Yuan Qingyan

This is a very common phenomenon. We deeply sympathize with Mr. Yuan and other friends in the same situation. This "boredom" is of the times and is unavoidable for every modern youth. Even if you don't read any books, you will naturally feel it sooner or later in the hardships of life. Mr. Yuan's boredom seems to prove the saying that the more knowledge one has, the more pain one experiences is correct. In fact, ignorance is truly painful, and true pain is unavoidable. Knowing the root of the pain, we should find ways to overcome this root; there is really no need to fear it or be bored by it. What use is boredom? Therefore, Mr. Yuan's boredom has little to do with whether he reads or not.

Although we sympathize with the root of Mr. Yuan's boredom, we dare not agree with Mr. Yuan's attitude, and we must point out that Mr. Yuan's attitude seems a bit like escaping reality. Because this is indeed a common mistake that young people currently make, we must openly discuss it with everyone, hoping that those who have made the same mistake will quickly correct themselves.

Generally speaking, young people tend to be somewhat emotional and cannot see the ugliness of society. Because of his simple mind, earnest attitude, lack of life experience, and eagerness for quick results, he is often easily angry and easily disappointed; he only has enthusiasm and no patience. For everything, he is always too enthusiastic at first, hoping for too much, only wanting smooth sailing and immediate success.

At the same time, he overestimates his own strength and does not see objective reality. Thus, all hopes and all attempts become fantasies suspended in the air, impractical. Naturally, he will inevitably run into obstacles and bad luck everywhere. When the obstacles are too severe and the bad luck is too great, he cannot help but retreat hastily, making him feel disheartened and listless. Those with weak wills may either go along with the ugliness or indulge in sex, love, or some kind of enjoyment, daring not open their eyes to see the world again. Those who are unwilling to degenerate but cannot coordinate with practice will naturally fall into extreme contradictory pain. His mind is constantly struggling and agonizing because it is separated from practice. His thoughts only develop in fantasy, becoming more and more isolated from reality, turning into someone who only knows how to talk big, act crazy, and cannot get along with the people around him. He feels no taste in life, does not like to work, does not want to work, and even feels that there is no one in the world who can talk to him, no one who can work with him. He develops hatred and suspicion towards everyone, rejects all friendship, and drives himself into loneliness day by day, shrinking his living space day by day, shrinking into a dead end. As a result, everyone is afraid of you when they see you, calling you crazy. After reaching this point, if you do not suddenly realize the consequences, you may go mad, insane, or commit suicide. If you reflect on your past enthusiasm for society, isn't it completely opposite now? If you ask yourself, you have been angry your whole life, even sacrificed your own life, what benefit has it brought to society? I think the answer must be heartbreaking. Now, how can we say benefit? We can only say that in some ways, we have helped the ugliness of society.

Here, Mr. Yuan, don't be offended, because this reply is not for Mr. Yuan alone. Mr. Yuan's condition is not as deep as described above. As long as Mr. Yuan turns around and corrects himself, Mr. Yuan still has a very optimistic future. Now, let's get back to the main topic and talk about Mr. Yuan's attitude towards occupation! (To be continued)

Triangular Inter-Port Swimming Closes: Tianjin Overwhelms Hong Kong to Win Championship 199

Scores: Tianjin 38, Hong Kong 34, Shanghai 27

Water Polo Final: Hong Kong Wins Over Shanghai 5-1

Last night was the final night of the Shanghai-Tianjin-Hong Kong triangular inter-port swimming competition. It was raining heavily, and the roads were flooded with several inches of water. However, more than a thousand spectators still went to the French Club, with Chinese accounting for only 1%. Mr. and Mrs. Wang Zhengting and Mr. and Mrs. Shen Silang were also present. Inspiring music was broadcast over the radio, just like the heavy rain, encouraging the athletes of the three ports to make their final efforts and compete for the championship.

Situation of Championship 200

In the previous two nights, Hong Kong had the advantage. Last night, at the beginning, in the first event, the 50-yard freestyle, Tianjin's Niniweiji took first place, and Puluodeng took third, adding 6 points. Shanghai's Haimengte was second, and Hong Kong failed to place. Tianjin then surpassed Hong Kong with a score of 27 to 24. In the second event, the 100-yard backstroke, Hong Kong's Liu Xiven lost to Tianjin's Woerwen, losing another 2 points. The score was 32 to 27. In the third event, diving, Shanghai took first and second place, Tianjin third, and Hong Kong was completely defeated again. The outcome depended on the 440-yard freestyle. Because Hong Kong was sure to win the water polo against Shanghai, gaining 3 points, the score would be 30 to 33, with Tianjin winning. If Hong Kong could get first and third place in the 440-yard freestyle, and Tianjin only got second, then each would get 36 points, tying for the championship. Therefore, a fierce battle ensued in this race. Lawrence and Nuomen competed most fiercely. In the end, Lawrence narrowly lost to Tianjin's Nuomen by half a body length. Luochaipiliela took third place. Hong Kong got 4 points, Tianjin 5 points. The total score was 38 to 34, and Tianjin won the championship. In the water polo result, Shanghai lost to Hong Kong 1 to 5. There were many fouls on both sides. Hong Kong's Lawrence was sent off twice, and Shanghai's Sinclair was also sent off once. Hong Kong's passing and shooting were excellent. Goalkeeper Chen Xipei's true skills were not seen because there were no dangerous shots. Shanghai's Bolattlei, originally a famous football player, was more skilled than Zhou Xianyan and saved many dangerous shots, worthy of the name "Iron Gate on Land and Water." Hong Kong's left defender, Fulage, could attack and defend, and was the fatal wound for the Shanghai team. The scores of the three teams are as follows:

Education News

Ministry of Education Orders Commemoration of September 18th Incident 217

The Ministry of Education telegraphed the education departments of various provinces and cities and all colleges and universities above the specialized level on the 14th, stating: "Recently, the Executive Yuan forwarded a telegram from the National Government instructing the Central Executive Committee, stating that the third anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation is approaching. The 137th regular meeting of the committee has stipulated the following commemorative measures: On this day, all banquets and entertainment nationwide will be suspended. Party, government, military, police organs, groups, and schools in various places will hold commemorative meetings separately. The senior party departments in each place will convene representative commemorative conferences from all walks of life. All party members, civil servants, schools, shops, and households will suspend work for five minutes at 11 am that morning, stand up in silence, and pledge to wipe out national humiliation, and express deep condolences to the soldiers who died resisting Japan and the compatriots who died in the disaster." Upon receiving this, it is ordered that all subordinates comply. Seal of the Ministry of Education, September 14th, 23rd year.

The Municipal People's Education Museum on Wenmiao Road in this city is preparing to commemorate the loss of the Northeast for three years. Because the lost territory has not been recovered and foreign aggression has not ended, a tragic and enthusiastic commemoration should be held on this day of national survival to promote public awareness. Therefore, a commemorative conference will be held in the lecture hall of the museum at 2 pm this afternoon. Prominent party and state figures will be invited to give speeches, and colleagues from the museum will perform a costumed speech "Blood Sacrifice" to awaken the public.

Central Government to Approve Confucius Memorial Song 223

This year, for Confucius's birthday, the Central Government, in order to carefully prepare a Confucius Memorial Song, ordered the Ministry of Education through the Executive Yuan to notify all levels of schools across the country that before a suitable lyric is prepared, the Confucius Memorial Song will be temporarily absent during the memorial ceremony. Later, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Education to prepare this memorial song so that it could be used during the Confucius memorial ceremony. Yesterday, the Executive Yuan, according to the Ministry of Education's presentation, proposed to use the passage "When the Great Way prevails, it will lead to Datong" from the Book of Rites, "The Great Learning," as the Confucius Memorial Song. The reason is that this passage is very in line with modern social thought and coincides with the purpose of the Three Principles of the People. The score already made by the National Conservatory of Music was also attached. It is said that the Central Government is reviewing this case and will soon issue an order for its adoption.

This City Convenes Meeting of Secondary School Deans of Students and Civics Teachers 224

Held yesterday at Wuben Girls' High School with over eighty schools represented

Commissioner Tao and Director Pan provided guidance on student guidance policies

The City Party Headquarters and the Municipal Bureau of Education convened a discussion meeting yesterday at 2:00 PM in the auditorium of Wuben Girls' High School. Deans of students and civics teachers from public and private secondary schools citywide were invited. Commissioner Tao of the City Party Headquarters and Director Pan of the Municipal Bureau of Education provided guidance on student guidance policies. The details are recorded as follows:

Attendees: In addition to Tao Baichuan, Standing Committee Member of the City Party Headquarters, Yu Zhongbiao, Director of the Party Affairs Education Division, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Education, and Chen Bai, Section Chief, attendees included over one hundred deans of students and civics teachers from over eighty schools, including Wuben, Jingye, Yangjing, Wusong, Nanshang, Junyi, Minli, Binhai, Minguang, Peiming, Aiqun, Aiguo, Xinlu, Chengzhong, Guangxia, Jinan, Shibei, Xinya, Zhengyi, Huadong, Shangzhong, Pudong, Daozhong, and Cihang, such as Zhu Ya Kui, Wang Longzhang, Xu Xingchu, Xu Zexiang, Zhou Shifu, Li Chongpu, Zhang Yongchun, Jin Yuezhang, Huang Daping, Chen Guangyu, and Wang Xuequan.

Chairman’s Report: Chairman Tao Baichuan first gave a report, stating that the mission of Party Affairs teachers and student guidance directors is very important and closely related to the Party Headquarters. Generally, not all teachers are Party members, but deans of students and civics teachers are all comrades of our Party. In the past, the Party Headquarters had not convened meetings with these comrades, leading to a lack of mutual connection. This is a deficiency. In the future, we want deans of students and Party Affairs teachers to develop a relationship with the Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Education. Therefore, we will regularly convene meetings for mutual discussion and exchange of ideas. The mission undertaken by everyone for secondary education in Shanghai is very important, especially in today's China. The responsibility of guiding middle school students is even more significant. Regarding the training of students, I think we can utilize the organization of student self-governance associations. However, the student movements of today are different from those of the May Fourth era. In the past, mass movements naturally included student movements, often leading the masses to abandon their professions. This was a major problem. Future student movements must absolutely not be like this. The organization of student self-governance associations must be based on the Three Principles of the People to train students in self-governed life within the school and to promote their intellectual, moral, physical, and communal development. Deans of students can utilize the organization of student self-governance associations to train students. At the same time, I hope everyone will first understand their own responsibilities, second, enrich their knowledge for the work they should possess, and cultivate their personality, so that they can perform their work competently and happily.

Director’s Speech: Director Pan then gave a speech, stating: (1) There should be a common trend in student guidance policies for secondary schools in Shanghai. Whether one is strict or lenient with students, education is not a private enterprise of one or two people. Therefore, although schools are divided into public and private, the work done by schools is the same. They are all engaged in educational work that is closely related to the nation and the people. Any school's dean of students and civics teacher is running on the same road in their management of students. Of course, when divided into stages within the educational system, elementary school, middle school, and university have different student guidance methods due to the age limits of the students being educated. However, secondary schools in the same stage must have a common trend. Otherwise, the level of strictness will vary greatly from school to school, with a great impact. The standard of whether it should be lenient or strict should be sought from comrades who are actually training students. (2) So, what should our trend ultimately be? In my personal opinion, any policy or trend cannot ignore the current environment of the country. After all, nothing can escape time and space. Therefore, to determine the student guidance trend for the secondary school stage, we cannot erase the current environment of China. The China of today is like a house surrounded by fire. Everyone inside is in danger of being burned to death. Now is not the time for us to jump into the fire pit; we are already in the fire pit. We should find a way to escape the fire pit. Education is the most fundamental method of national salvation among many methods of national salvation. Hu Shi once said that everyone says education is bankrupt, but to save a bankrupt country, we still rely on education. Therefore, people in the education field should take more responsibility. In the context of time and space for secondary education, we cannot allow students to be permissive and free. Student movements have been a good term since the May Fourth Movement, but since the two major blows of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, it has become clear that our students lack perseverance and only have impulsiveness. This cannot save the country. Now, students with calmer minds have realized this. This is the beginning of a turning point. At this moment, talking about student movements obviously cannot be like it was during the May Fourth Movement. Previously, it was destructive work; now we want to build. Therefore, we can no longer be permissive with middle school students. However, only the dean of students can train schools to conduct student movements in middle schools. Only civics teachers can assist the dean of students in doing so. All student actions, speech, and thoughts must be guided by the dean of students and civics teachers. Deans of students and civics teachers are entrusted by the Party and the government to take on this important responsibility. I hope everyone understands this point and trains students to become individuals who can save themselves in the future. (3) Now, if we analyze the responsibilities for the student unrest in many schools, one-third is the responsibility of the students, one-third is the responsibility of some teachers and staff who incite the unrest, and another one-third should be the responsibility of all teachers and staff from the principal down. If every teacher and staff member in the school, from the principal down, does not neglect their duties, then the students will have no loopholes to exploit. It will be easier for the dean of students and civics teachers to train students. Otherwise, if the school itself is not sound in all aspects and the teachers and staff do not fulfill their duties, then the dean of students and civics teachers will not be able to train students. However, even if everyone encounters this difficult environment, they should still work hard. However, you must obtain the principal's understanding. The principal must also take responsibility for student guidance. Finally, one more point is very important. The dean of students and civics teachers are not nominal positions and cannot hold concurrent jobs. They must actually go to the school to take responsibility. The prevalent symptom now is that most deans of students and civics teachers have taken on the title but do not take responsibility. This will cause the student management of secondary schools in Shanghai to be entirely ruined by the deans of students and civics teachers. In the future, the Bureau of Education will send personnel to each school at any time to investigate. If they encounter this kind of irresponsible dean of students or civics teacher, they will definitely not be allowed to hold the position. For the sake of secondary schools and secondary education in Shanghai, we must rescue those who are specially responsible and have them take responsibility.

Municipal Bureau of Education Sends Personnel to Investigate the Situation of Science Teachers in Primary and Secondary Schools 225

Departure set for the 17th, completion of investigation within one week

The Municipal Bureau of Education previously received an order from the Ministry of Education to organize a summer workshop for science teachers in secondary schools in this city to provide science teachers in various secondary schools in this city with opportunities for professional development, improve the efficiency of science teaching in various schools, and improve students' science proficiency. It also aimed to remedy the drawbacks of middle school students in this city performing poorly in science subjects in past national examinations. However, after investigation, only over 120 science teachers in various secondary schools in this city have received this training. There are still a significant number of people who have not received training due to various reasons, and there is inevitably a distinction between good and bad. Furthermore, the hiring of science teachers in various schools is often done hastily and with unqualified people filling positions, which has a significant impact on students' science proficiency. Therefore, the Bureau attaches importance to science facilities in secondary schools and has decided to investigate the situation of science teachers in secondary schools in this semester in order to make distinctions. It is heard that the Bureau has already assigned Shen E, Du Xi, Xu Guiji, Sheng Youxuan, Shen Wuguang, Lu Hanqiu, Chen Yu and other seven people to depart tomorrow (the 17th) to go to various schools to conduct on-site investigations, which are expected to be completed within one week.

Vocational Education Society’s Vocational Guidance Center Issues Letter to School Youths Yesterday 226

Willing to provide guidance and service to young people when difficulties arise in selecting subjects and seeking education

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center of the China Vocational Education Society, considering that when schools in this city and other regions recently started classes, and when new students or students already enrolled selected subjects and sought education, they often encountered difficulties that needed to be resolved but had no place to ask for advice, since the center has the responsibility of guiding young people, it is willing to provide services to young people. Yesterday, it issued a letter to school youths, the original text of which is as follows: Time flies, another academic year has passed. My respectable and lovable young students, you are once again burying yourselves in your studies and living your school lives. Some of you are continuing your previous work, carrying on past achievements, while others have just completed one stage and are entering a new school. We witness the panic of the times and are alarmed by the difficulties of finding a way out. Learning from past mistakes, we are even more apprehensive. Instead of panicking when things happen, why not fix things before they occur? Considering that young people in various schools may feel doubts and discomfort at the beginning of this academic year, they may feel that the subjects they have chosen do not match their personality, or that the courses they are currently taking do not arouse their interest, or they may doubt whether the subject they have chosen is suitable for their needs, or they may fear that their personal financial resources will not be enough to complete their studies, or they may have entered school rashly due to temporary emotions and seem to regret it, or they may want to learn widely because of the encouragement of friends, but are hesitant. In addition, individual health may have shortcomings, and family affairs may need to be resolved. All these concerns will inevitably distract you. If you lack the guidance and solutions, you may not be able to dispel your doubts and feel at ease. Our center has a heart to help and a responsibility to guide. We are not overestimating ourselves and are willing to provide consultations for young people and are happy to discuss with students. We hope that our opinions, even if they are not profound, can prevent you from getting lost. If students in various schools have any doubts or difficulties in the future, they can ask questions in person or by mail, and we will be happy to answer them. If our answers are inappropriate or unsatisfactory, we hope that experts will correct our deficiencies. We would be very pleased.

Wuzhou Pharmacy Offers Preferential Treatment to Schools Purchasing Medications for Tuberculosis 227

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education yesterday issued an instruction to the elementary schools in this city, stating: According to a letter approved from Wuzhou Pharmacy, "Upon investigation, tuberculosis is widespread globally, and its harm is unmatched. Eastern nations, in particular, have a predisposition to infection. Now that our country is experiencing economic decline and hardship, the spread of infection is even more conceivable. Therefore, various groups in Shanghai have organized tuberculosis prevention associations to popularize common knowledge of prevention and promote early treatment, which is a crucial and urgent measure to save the nation. We recently learned that your bureau, with the assistance of the China Red Cross Children's Section, conducted examinations in elementary schools such as Bide and Xicheng in this city, and the results of the examinations showed that 60-70% of the children had positive reactions. Your bureau has taken measures to provide treatment according to the severity of the cases, demonstrating the educational authorities' utmost concern for the health of students and the nation. Our company operates in new medicines, which is part of the health industry. We should do our best to help within our capabilities. In addition to donating 500 yuan to help the academic community treat tuberculosis, we have specially formulated preferential measures for medications used in treatment, as recorded below. We do not dare to be generous; we are merely fulfilling our duty." A copy of the preferential measures for medications used in the treatment of tuberculosis is attached. Upon approval, it is found that tuberculosis testing and vaccinations in this city have attracted attention from all sectors since they were first carried out last year. This year, we will continue to carry them out. All weak children and children who have been diagnosed with pulmonary tuberculosis in various schools should immediately contact the children and seek treatment as soon as possible. The medications for the treatment of tuberculosis manufactured by the pharmacy can be handled in accordance with the preferential rules issued by the pharmacy. It is urgent to copy the preferential measures and order the elementary schools to follow them. This order is attached with a copy of the preferential measures for medications used in the treatment of tuberculosis manufactured by Wuzhou Pharmacy. (1) These measures are limited to the purchase of medications for the treatment of tuberculosis by elementary school students in this city. (2) Our company has printed preferential certificates and distributed them to various elementary schools. After verification, they can be used to purchase medications from our company at 4th Malu. (3) Our company's self-made products, such as Globe Brand Malt Extract Cod Liver Oil, Wuzhou Milky White Cod Liver Oil, and Cough Syrup, will all be reduced by half. (4) Doctor's prescriptions will only be charged at cost. (5) Other injection medicines will be provided by our company without additional fees. (6) These measures will be valid for one year, from September 1, 1934 to August 31, 1935. They will be invalid after the expiration date.

The Newcomer Weekly, a Rising Force, to be Published Tomorrow 229

Considering that in recent years, young people in this city's education circles tend to focus on the study of classroom textbooks, while remaining ignorant of common sense in daily applications, social situations, international realities, etc., and in order to correct these shortcomings, prominent figures in the education circles feel that there is a need to publish a supplementary reading material for young people. Therefore, Tong Xingyou, Zhao Yuanan, and others have initiated the publication of a Newcomer Weekly, which is specifically for general young people and housewives to read. The content focuses on the inculcation of knowledge, ideological training, and moral cultivation, while striving for the interestingness of writing skills. The authors are all contemporary celebrities and experts, such as Chen Bulei, Pan Gongzhan, Zhou Fohai, Liu Zhanen, Tao Baichuan, Fan Zhongyun, Fu Donghua, Xie Liuyi, Yang Weiyu, Pan Yangyao, Li Gongpu, and other two or thirty people. It is heard that the presidents of various universities and middle schools believe that this publication is closely related to guiding young people, and all want to set up distribution points in their respective schools to facilitate young people's purchase and reading. Therefore, in two days, more than 2,000 subscriptions have been arranged with the agency. The book is sold through the Life Bookstore, and subscriptions are handled by the Shanghai Bank Ximen Branch. Details can be found in tomorrow's newspaper.

Future American Cotton Prices 244

Will Fluctuate Between 12 and 15 Cents

A New York telegram on September 14th reported on the cotton market situation for the week, stating that at the beginning of the week, the cotton market reacted after the release of the Department of Agriculture report and the liquidation of long positions, as well as the accumulated short positions from the previous week. However, when the December futures price approached 13 cents, buying interest increased significantly, as this price was close to the government's loan standard for cotton farmers. In the middle of the week, there was first a rally due to short covering and retail purchases, followed by a fall due to poor labor unrest and renewed liquidation by long investors. Yarn mill demand has sharply reduced due to strikes, so futures buyers are maintaining a 12-cent loan to curb the pressure of new cotton entering the market. The new cotton that has already entered the market has been absorbed to fulfill old contracts, but after the price increase, buyers are wary. Those with cotton on hand can obtain a 12-cent loan by pledging their cotton at a price of 15 cents or higher in New Orleans. It is expected that if the 12-cent loan can effectively prevent the cotton price from falling, then the world cotton market will have higher prices, so future transactions will fluctuate between 15 and 12 cents. Cotton trading this week has been quite slow due to textile labor unrest.

Grain and Flour Futures Business Was Offset Trading 246

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed a pattern of first falling and then stabilizing. Foreign wheat prices in Chicago fell by around 7-9 cents, and Canadian wheat fell by around 4-5 cents. Market sentiment was weak at the opening, and the current month fell to a low of 2.36 yuan. Distant months also fell by 1-1.5 cents compared to the previous day. However, each mill felt that its margin stakes were already substantial and had no intention of increasing them further. At most, the inland buyers mainly held long positions. Under these circumstances, it was very difficult to exit, so they had to endure, and the market stabilized and rebounded. By the afternoon opening, trading for each month was still quiet, with only minor offset trading by the mills and little activity. As a result, the current month improved by 0.5%, October remained unchanged, October improved by 0.25%, December fell by 0.5%, January fell by 0.5%, and February fell by 0.5%.

Autumn Rain Damages Silkworm Season 256

In the townships of 杭县(Hangxian), this year's autumn silkworm rearing has been hampered by the drought. Although supervisors advised and guided supplemental late silkworm rearing, the amount was still not robust. Early silkworms had a large quantity of lush leaves and were ready to spin cocoons. The late silkworms were opening leaves for the third molt, but since the beginning of autumn, there has been continuous heavy rain, causing sudden changes in the silkworms that ate rain-soaked leaves. Early silkworms with lush leaves were found to have jaundice, and early silkworms also had stagnant leaves and lost sleep. A bumper harvest is unlikely.

Oil Market Asphalt Price Fluctuates After Rise 257

The asphalt market in autumn was extremely prosperous. Since the beginning of autumn, its momentum reached a peak for a time, mainly because the supply in Hankou was insufficient, while buyers flocked to the market. Therefore, a month ago, the market price soared by two yuan. In addition, there was a severe drought in western Zhejiang, and the asphalt yield from cypress trees was only 20-30% of a normal year. Consequently, asphalt from Jiaxing was particularly expensive, jumping from 17 yuan per load to 20 yuan. However, there was no real demand, and the price increase was entirely driven by speculation, which is truly unbelievable. Recently, however, the weather has gradually cooled, and goods from Hankou have gradually arrived. Surprisingly, the market has become more sluggish than in early autumn. As a result, high-quality Jing asphalt from Hankou, which had risen to over 16 yuan per piece, has recently fallen back to around 15 yuan. Asphalt from Macheng has also fallen from 16 yuan to below 15 yuan. This shows that although inventory is scarce and the yield is low, demand is not as strong as in previous years. Therefore, although prices rose, they could not be sustained and had to fall back down. Currently, the local inventory is still very low, but sales are unusually slow. Since the Hankou market has fallen, the local market will naturally follow suit. Traders are offering high-quality Jing asphalt at 19 yuan per piece, ordinary Jing asphalt at 18.4 yuan, and Macheng asphalt at 16.45 yuan.
